        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1><a id="user-content-airbnb-javascript-style-guide-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#airbnb-javascript-style-guide-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Airbnb JavaScript Style Guide() {</h1>
<p><em>A mostly reasonable approach to JavaScript</em></p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Note</strong>: this guide assumes you are using <a href="https://babeljs.io" rel="nofollow">Babel</a>, and requires that you use <a href="https://npmjs.com/babel-preset-airbnb" rel="nofollow">babel-preset-airbnb</a> or the equivalent. It also assumes you are installing shims/polyfills in your app, with <a href="https://npmjs.com/airbnb-browser-shims" rel="nofollow">airbnb-browser-shims</a> or the equivalent.</p>
</blockquote>
<p><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/eslint-config-airbnb" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a933cce640ac4a82eadf6bba106e1523b12c8e1dd8e8dc4b8754d6b555c18615/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6e706d2f646d2f65736c696e742d636f6e6669672d616972626e622e737667" alt="Downloads" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/npm/dm/eslint-config-airbnb.svg" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
<a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/eslint-config-airbnb-base" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/eec211cbd52a6227ef09a18a19bdd49234ce48e395a383bfbfedeaf6c5052d33/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6e706d2f646d2f65736c696e742d636f6e6669672d616972626e622d626173652e737667" alt="Downloads" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/npm/dm/eslint-config-airbnb-base.svg" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
<a href="https://gitter.im/airbnb/javascript?utm_source=badge&amp;utm_medium=badge&amp;utm_campaign=pr-badge" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/5dbac0213da25c445bd11f168587c11a200ba153ef3014e8408e462e410169b3/68747470733a2f2f6261646765732e6769747465722e696d2f4a6f696e253230436861742e737667" alt="Gitter" data-canonical-src="https://badges.gitter.im/Join%20Chat.svg" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>

<h2><a id="user-content-types" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#types"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Types</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-types--primitives"></a><a name="user-content-1.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#types--primitives">1.1</a> <strong>Primitives</strong>: When you access a primitive type you work directly on its value.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>string</code></li>
<li><code>number</code></li>
<li><code>boolean</code></li>
<li><code>null</code></li>
<li><code>undefined</code></li>
<li><code>symbol</code></li>
<li><code>bigint</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const foo = 1;
let bar = foo;

bar = 9;

console.log(foo, bar); // =&gt; 1, 9
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">9</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 1, 9</span></pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Symbols and BigInts cannot be faithfully polyfilled, so they should not be used when targeting browsers/environments that don’t support them natively.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-types--complex"></a><a name="user-content-1.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#types--complex">1.2</a>  <strong>Complex</strong>: When you access a complex type you work on a reference to its value.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>object</code></li>
<li><code>array</code></li>
<li><code>function</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const foo = [1, 2];
const bar = foo;

bar[0] = 9;

console.log(foo[0], bar[0]); // =&gt; 9, 9
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">9</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 9, 9</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-references" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#references"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>References</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-references--prefer-const"></a><a name="user-content-2.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#references--prefer-const">2.1</a> Use <code>const</code> for all of your references; avoid using <code>var</code>. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-const.html" rel="nofollow"><code>prefer-const</code></a>, <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-const-assign.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-const-assign</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? This ensures that you can’t reassign your references, which can lead to bugs and difficult to comprehend code.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
var a = 1;
var b = 2;

// good
const a = 1;
const b = 2;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-references--disallow-var"></a><a name="user-content-2.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#references--disallow-var">2.2</a> If you must reassign references, use <code>let</code> instead of <code>var</code>. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-var.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-var</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? <code>let</code> is block-scoped rather than function-scoped like <code>var</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
var count = 1;
if (true) {
  count += 1;
}

// good, use the let.
let count = 1;
if (true) {
  count += 1;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">count</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">count</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good, use the let.</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">count</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">count</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-references--block-scope"></a><a name="user-content-2.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#references--block-scope">2.3</a> Note that both <code>let</code> and <code>const</code> are block-scoped, whereas <code>var</code> is function-scoped.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// const and let only exist in the blocks they are defined in.
{
  let a = 1;
  const b = 1;
  var c = 1;
}
console.log(a); // ReferenceError
console.log(b); // ReferenceError
console.log(c); // Prints 1
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// const and let only exist in the blocks they are defined in.</span>
<span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// ReferenceError</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// ReferenceError</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// Prints 1</span></pre></div>
<p>In the above code, you can see that referencing <code>a</code> and <code>b</code> will produce a ReferenceError, while <code>c</code> contains the number. This is because <code>a</code> and <code>b</code> are block scoped, while <code>c</code> is scoped to the containing function.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-objects" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#objects"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Objects</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-objects--no-new"></a><a name="user-content-3.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#objects--no-new">3.1</a> Use the literal syntax for object creation. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-new-object.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-new-object</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const item = new Object();

// good
const item = {};
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">item</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">item</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-es6-computed-properties"></a><a name="user-content-3.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#es6-computed-properties">3.2</a> Use computed property names when creating objects with dynamic property names.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? They allow you to define all the properties of an object in one place.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="
function getKey(k) {
  return `a key named ${k}`;
}

// bad
const obj = {
  id: 5,
  name: 'San Francisco',
};
obj[getKey('enabled')] = true;

// good
const obj = {
  id: 5,
  name: 'San Francisco',
  [getKey('enabled')]: true,
};
"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getKey</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">k</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">`a key named <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">k</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">'San Francisco'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-en">getKey</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'enabled'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">'San Francisco'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-en">getKey</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'enabled'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-es6-object-shorthand"></a><a name="user-content-3.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#es6-object-shorthand">3.3</a> Use object method shorthand. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/object-shorthand.html" rel="nofollow"><code>object-shorthand</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const atom = {
  value: 1,

  addValue: function (value) {
    return atom.value + value;
  },
};

// good
const atom = {
  value: 1,

  addValue(value) {
    return atom.value + value;
  },
};
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">atom</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">value</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

  <span class="pl-en">addValue</span>: <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">atom</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">atom</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">value</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

  <span class="pl-en">addValue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">atom</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-es6-object-concise"></a><a name="user-content-3.6"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#es6-object-concise">3.4</a> Use property value shorthand. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/object-shorthand.html" rel="nofollow"><code>object-shorthand</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? It is shorter and descriptive.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const lukeSkywalker = 'Luke Skywalker';

// bad
const obj = {
  lukeSkywalker: lukeSkywalker,
};

// good
const obj = {
  lukeSkywalker,
};
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">lukeSkywalker</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Luke Skywalker'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">lukeSkywalker</span>: <span class="pl-s1">lukeSkywalker</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  lukeSkywalker<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-objects--grouped-shorthand"></a><a name="user-content-3.7"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#objects--grouped-shorthand">3.5</a> Group your shorthand properties at the beginning of your object declaration.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? It’s easier to tell which properties are using the shorthand.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const anakinSkywalker = 'Anakin Skywalker';
const lukeSkywalker = 'Luke Skywalker';

// bad
const obj = {
  episodeOne: 1,
  twoJediWalkIntoACantina: 2,
  lukeSkywalker,
  episodeThree: 3,
  mayTheFourth: 4,
  anakinSkywalker,
};

// good
const obj = {
  lukeSkywalker,
  anakinSkywalker,
  episodeOne: 1,
  twoJediWalkIntoACantina: 2,
  episodeThree: 3,
  mayTheFourth: 4,
};
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">anakinSkywalker</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Anakin Skywalker'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">lukeSkywalker</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Luke Skywalker'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">episodeOne</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">twoJediWalkIntoACantina</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  lukeSkywalker<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">episodeThree</span>: <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">mayTheFourth</span>: <span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  anakinSkywalker<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  lukeSkywalker<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  anakinSkywalker<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">episodeOne</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">twoJediWalkIntoACantina</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">episodeThree</span>: <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">mayTheFourth</span>: <span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-objects--quoted-props"></a><a name="user-content-3.8"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#objects--quoted-props">3.6</a> Only quote properties that are invalid identifiers. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/quote-props.html" rel="nofollow"><code>quote-props</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? In general we consider it subjectively easier to read. It improves syntax highlighting, and is also more easily optimized by many JS engines.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const bad = {
  'foo': 3,
  'bar': 4,
  'data-blah': 5,
};

// good
const good = {
  foo: 3,
  bar: 4,
  'data-blah': 5,
};
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bad</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span>: <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'bar'</span>: <span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'data-blah'</span>: <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">good</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">foo</span>: <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">bar</span>: <span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'data-blah'</span>: <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-objects--prototype-builtins"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#objects--prototype-builtins">3.7</a> Do not call <code>Object.prototype</code> methods directly, such as <code>hasOwnProperty</code>, <code>propertyIsEnumerable</code>, and <code>isPrototypeOf</code>. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-prototype-builtins" rel="nofollow"><code>no-prototype-builtins</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? These methods may be shadowed by properties on the object in question - consider <code>{ hasOwnProperty: false }</code> - or, the object may be a null object (<code>Object.create(null)</code>).</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
console.log(object.hasOwnProperty(key));

// good
console.log(Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(object, key));

// best
const has = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty; // cache the lookup once, in module scope.
console.log(has.call(object, key));
/* or */
import has from 'has'; // https://www.npmjs.com/package/has
console.log(has(object, key));
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">hasOwnProperty</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">hasOwnProperty</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">object</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">has</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">hasOwnProperty</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// cache the lookup once, in module scope.</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">has</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">object</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c">/* or */</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">has</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'has'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// https://www.npmjs.com/package/has</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">has</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">object</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-objects--rest-spread"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#objects--rest-spread">3.8</a> Prefer the object spread syntax over <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object/assign" rel="nofollow"><code>Object.assign</code></a> to shallow-copy objects. Use the object rest operator to get a new object with certain properties omitted. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-object-spread" rel="nofollow"><code>prefer-object-spread</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// very bad
const original = { a: 1, b: 2 };
const copy = Object.assign(original, { c: 3 }); // this mutates `original` ಠ_ಠ
delete copy.a; // so does this

// bad
const original = { a: 1, b: 2 };
const copy = Object.assign({}, original, { c: 3 }); // copy =&gt; { a: 1, b: 2, c: 3 }

// good
const original = { a: 1, b: 2 };
const copy = { ...original, c: 3 }; // copy =&gt; { a: 1, b: 2, c: 3 }

const { a, ...noA } = copy; // noA =&gt; { b: 2, c: 3 }
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// very bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">original</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">a</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">b</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">copy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">assign</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">original</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">c</span>: <span class="pl-c1">3</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// this mutates `original` ಠ_ಠ</span>
<span class="pl-k">delete</span> <span class="pl-s1">copy</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// so does this</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">original</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">a</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">b</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">copy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">assign</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">original</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">c</span>: <span class="pl-c1">3</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// copy =&gt; { a: 1, b: 2, c: 3 }</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">original</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">a</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">b</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">copy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> ...<span class="pl-s1">original</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">c</span>: <span class="pl-c1">3</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// copy =&gt; { a: 1, b: 2, c: 3 }</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> a<span class="pl-kos">,</span> ...<span class="pl-s1">noA</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">copy</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// noA =&gt; { b: 2, c: 3 }</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-arrays" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#arrays"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Arrays</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-arrays--literals"></a><a name="user-content-4.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrays--literals">4.1</a> Use the literal syntax for array creation. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-array-constructor.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-array-constructor</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const items = new Array();

// good
const items = [];
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">items</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Array</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">items</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrays--push"></a><a name="user-content-4.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrays--push">4.2</a> Use <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Array/push" rel="nofollow">Array#push</a> instead of direct assignment to add items to an array.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const someStack = [];

// bad
someStack[someStack.length] = 'abracadabra';

// good
someStack.push('abracadabra');
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">someStack</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-s1">someStack</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">someStack</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'abracadabra'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-s1">someStack</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">push</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'abracadabra'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-es6-array-spreads"></a><a name="user-content-4.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#es6-array-spreads">4.3</a> Use array spreads <code>...</code> to copy arrays.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const len = items.length;
const itemsCopy = [];
let i;

for (i = 0; i &lt; len; i += 1) {
  itemsCopy[i] = items[i];
}

// good
const itemsCopy = [...items];
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">len</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">items</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">itemsCopy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">len</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">itemsCopy</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">items</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">itemsCopy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>...<span class="pl-s1">items</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrays--from"></a>
<a name="user-content-arrays--from-iterable"></a><a name="user-content-4.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrays--from-iterable">4.4</a> To convert an iterable object to an array, use spreads <code>...</code> instead of <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Array/from" rel="nofollow"><code>Array.from</code></a>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const foo = document.querySelectorAll('.foo');

// good
const nodes = Array.from(foo);

// best
const nodes = [...foo];
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">document</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">querySelectorAll</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Array</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">from</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>...<span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrays--from-array-like"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrays--from-array-like">4.5</a> Use <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Array/from" rel="nofollow"><code>Array.from</code></a> for converting an array-like object to an array.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const arrLike = { 0: 'foo', 1: 'bar', 2: 'baz', length: 3 };

// bad
const arr = Array.prototype.slice.call(arrLike);

// good
const arr = Array.from(arrLike);
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">arrLike</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>: <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>: <span class="pl-s">'bar'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>: <span class="pl-s">'baz'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">length</span>: <span class="pl-c1">3</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Array</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">slice</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">arrLike</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Array</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">from</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">arrLike</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrays--mapping"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrays--mapping">4.6</a> Use <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Array/from" rel="nofollow"><code>Array.from</code></a> instead of spread <code>...</code> for mapping over iterables, because it avoids creating an intermediate array.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const baz = [...foo].map(bar);

// good
const baz = Array.from(foo, bar);
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">baz</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>...<span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">baz</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Array</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">from</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrays--callback-return"></a><a name="user-content-4.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrays--callback-return">4.7</a> Use return statements in array method callbacks. It’s ok to omit the return if the function body consists of a single statement returning an expression without side effects, following <a href="#arrows--implicit-return">8.2</a>. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/array-callback-return" rel="nofollow"><code>array-callback-return</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// good
[1, 2, 3].map((x) =&gt; {
  const y = x + 1;
  return x * y;
});

// good
[1, 2, 3].map((x) =&gt; x + 1);

// bad - no returned value means `acc` becomes undefined after the first iteration
[[0, 1], [2, 3], [4, 5]].reduce((acc, item, index) =&gt; {
  const flatten = acc.concat(item);
});

// good
[[0, 1], [2, 3], [4, 5]].reduce((acc, item, index) =&gt; {
  const flatten = acc.concat(item);
  return flatten;
});

// bad
inbox.filter((msg) =&gt; {
  const { subject, author } = msg;
  if (subject === 'Mockingbird') {
    return author === 'Harper Lee';
  } else {
    return false;
  }
});

// good
inbox.filter((msg) =&gt; {
  const { subject, author } = msg;
  if (subject === 'Mockingbird') {
    return author === 'Harper Lee';
  }

  return false;
});
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad - no returned value means `acc` becomes undefined after the first iteration</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">reduce</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">acc</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">index</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">flatten</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">acc</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">concat</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">reduce</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">acc</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">index</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">flatten</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">acc</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">concat</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">flatten</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-s1">inbox</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">msg</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> subject<span class="pl-kos">,</span> author <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">msg</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">subject</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'Mockingbird'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">author</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'Harper Lee'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-s1">inbox</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">msg</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> subject<span class="pl-kos">,</span> author <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">msg</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">subject</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'Mockingbird'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">author</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'Harper Lee'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrays--bracket-newline"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrays--bracket-newline">4.8</a> Use line breaks after open and before close array brackets if an array has multiple lines</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const arr = [
  [0, 1], [2, 3], [4, 5],
];

const objectInArray = [{
  id: 1,
}, {
  id: 2,
}];

const numberInArray = [
  1, 2,
];

// good
const arr = [[0, 1], [2, 3], [4, 5]];

const objectInArray = [
  {
    id: 1,
  },
  {
    id: 2,
  },
];

const numberInArray = [
  1,
  2,
];
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">objectInArray</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">numberInArray</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">objectInArray</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">numberInArray</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-destructuring" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#destructuring"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Destructuring</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-destructuring--object"></a><a name="user-content-5.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#destructuring--object">5.1</a> Use object destructuring when accessing and using multiple properties of an object. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-destructuring" rel="nofollow"><code>prefer-destructuring</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Destructuring saves you from creating temporary references for those properties, and from repetitive access of the object. Repeating object access creates more repetitive code, requires more reading, and creates more opportunities for mistakes. Destructuring objects also provides a single site of definition of the object structure that is used in the block, rather than requiring reading the entire block to determine what is used.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function getFullName(user) {
  const firstName = user.firstName;
  const lastName = user.lastName;

  return `${firstName} ${lastName}`;
}

// good
function getFullName(user) {
  const { firstName, lastName } = user;
  return `${firstName} ${lastName}`;
}

// best
function getFullName({ firstName, lastName }) {
  return `${firstName} ${lastName}`;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getFullName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">user</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">firstName</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">user</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">lastName</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">user</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">`<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getFullName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">user</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> firstName<span class="pl-kos">,</span> lastName <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">user</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">`<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getFullName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> firstName<span class="pl-kos">,</span> lastName <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">`<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-destructuring--array"></a><a name="user-content-5.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#destructuring--array">5.2</a> Use array destructuring. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-destructuring" rel="nofollow"><code>prefer-destructuring</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const arr = [1, 2, 3, 4];

// bad
const first = arr[0];
const second = arr[1];

// good
const [first, second] = arr;
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">first</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">second</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">first</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">second</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-destructuring--object-over-array"></a><a name="user-content-5.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#destructuring--object-over-array">5.3</a> Use object destructuring for multiple return values, not array destructuring.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? You can add new properties over time or change the order of things without breaking call sites.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function processInput(input) {
  // then a miracle occurs
  return [left, right, top, bottom];
}

// the caller needs to think about the order of return data
const [left, __, top] = processInput(input);

// good
function processInput(input) {
  // then a miracle occurs
  return { left, right, top, bottom };
}

// the caller selects only the data they need
const { left, top } = processInput(input);
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">processInput</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">input</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// then a miracle occurs</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">left</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">right</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">top</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">bottom</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// the caller needs to think about the order of return data</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">left</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">__</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">top</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">processInput</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">input</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">processInput</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">input</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// then a miracle occurs</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> left<span class="pl-kos">,</span> right<span class="pl-kos">,</span> top<span class="pl-kos">,</span> bottom <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// the caller selects only the data they need</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> left<span class="pl-kos">,</span> top <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">processInput</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">input</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-strings" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#strings"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Strings</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-strings--quotes"></a><a name="user-content-6.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#strings--quotes">6.1</a> Use single quotes <code>''</code> for strings. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/quotes.html" rel="nofollow"><code>quotes</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const name = &quot;Capt. Janeway&quot;;

// bad - template literals should contain interpolation or newlines
const name = `Capt. Janeway`;

// good
const name = 'Capt. Janeway';
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"Capt. Janeway"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad - template literals should contain interpolation or newlines</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">`Capt. Janeway`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Capt. Janeway'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-strings--line-length"></a><a name="user-content-6.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#strings--line-length">6.2</a> Strings that cause the line to go over 100 characters should not be written across multiple lines using string concatenation.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Broken strings are painful to work with and make code less searchable.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const errorMessage = 'This is a super long error that was thrown because \
of Batman. When you stop to think about how Batman had anything to do \
with this, you would get nowhere \
fast.';

// bad
const errorMessage = 'This is a super long error that was thrown because ' +
  'of Batman. When you stop to think about how Batman had anything to do ' +
  'with this, you would get nowhere fast.';

// good
const errorMessage = 'This is a super long error that was thrown because of Batman. When you stop to think about how Batman had anything to do with this, you would get nowhere fast.';
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">errorMessage</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'This is a super long error that was thrown because \</span>
<span class="pl-s">of Batman. When you stop to think about how Batman had anything to do \</span>
<span class="pl-s">with this, you would get nowhere \</span>
<span class="pl-s">fast.'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">errorMessage</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'This is a super long error that was thrown because '</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'of Batman. When you stop to think about how Batman had anything to do '</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'with this, you would get nowhere fast.'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">errorMessage</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'This is a super long error that was thrown because of Batman. When you stop to think about how Batman had anything to do with this, you would get nowhere fast.'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-es6-template-literals"></a><a name="user-content-6.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#es6-template-literals">6.3</a> When programmatically building up strings, use template strings instead of concatenation. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-template.html" rel="nofollow"><code>prefer-template</code></a> <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/template-curly-spacing" rel="nofollow"><code>template-curly-spacing</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Template strings give you a readable, concise syntax with proper newlines and string interpolation features.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function sayHi(name) {
  return 'How are you, ' + name + '?';
}

// bad
function sayHi(name) {
  return ['How are you, ', name, '?'].join();
}

// bad
function sayHi(name) {
  return `How are you, ${ name }?`;
}

// good
function sayHi(name) {
  return `How are you, ${name}?`;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">sayHi</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">'How are you, '</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s">'?'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">sayHi</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'How are you, '</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'?'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">join</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">sayHi</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">`How are you, <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>?`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">sayHi</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">`How are you, <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>?`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-strings--eval"></a><a name="user-content-6.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#strings--eval">6.4</a> Never use <code>eval()</code> on a string, it opens too many vulnerabilities. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-eval" rel="nofollow"><code>no-eval</code></a></li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-strings--escaping"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#strings--escaping">6.5</a> Do not unnecessarily escape characters in strings. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-useless-escape" rel="nofollow"><code>no-useless-escape</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Backslashes harm readability, thus they should only be present when necessary.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const foo = '\'this\' \i\s \&quot;quoted\&quot;';

// good
const foo = '\'this\' is &quot;quoted&quot;';
const foo = `my name is '${name}'`;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'\'this\' \i\s \"quoted\"'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'\'this\' is "quoted"'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">`my name is '<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>'`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-functions" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#functions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Functions</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--declarations"></a><a name="user-content-7.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--declarations">7.1</a> Use named function expressions instead of function declarations. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/func-style" rel="nofollow"><code>func-style</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Function declarations are hoisted, which means that it’s easy - too easy - to reference the function before it is defined in the file. This harms readability and maintainability. If you find that a function’s definition is large or complex enough that it is interfering with understanding the rest of the file, then perhaps it’s time to extract it to its own module! Don’t forget to explicitly name the expression, regardless of whether or not the name is inferred from the containing variable (which is often the case in modern browsers or when using compilers such as Babel). This eliminates any assumptions made about the Error’s call stack. (<a href="https://github.com/airbnb/javascript/issues/794">Discussion</a>)</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function foo() {
  // ...
}

// bad
const foo = function () {
  // ...
};

// good
// lexical name distinguished from the variable-referenced invocation(s)
const short = function longUniqueMoreDescriptiveLexicalFoo() {
  // ...
};
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-c">// lexical name distinguished from the variable-referenced invocation(s)</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">short</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">longUniqueMoreDescriptiveLexicalFoo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--iife"></a><a name="user-content-7.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--iife">7.2</a> Wrap immediately invoked function expressions in parentheses. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/wrap-iife.html" rel="nofollow"><code>wrap-iife</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? An immediately invoked function expression is a single unit - wrapping both it, and its invocation parens, in parens, cleanly expresses this. Note that in a world with modules everywhere, you almost never need an IIFE.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// immediately-invoked function expression (IIFE)
(function () {
  console.log('Welcome to the Internet. Please follow me.');
}());
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// immediately-invoked function expression (IIFE)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Welcome to the Internet. Please follow me.'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--in-blocks"></a><a name="user-content-7.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#functions--in-blocks">7.3</a> Never declare a function in a non-function block (<code>if</code>, <code>while</code>, etc). Assign the function to a variable instead. Browsers will allow you to do it, but they all interpret it differently, which is bad news bears. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-loop-func.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-loop-func</code></a></li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--note-on-blocks"></a><a name="user-content-7.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--note-on-blocks">7.4</a> <strong>Note:</strong> ECMA-262 defines a <code>block</code> as a list of statements. A function declaration is not a statement.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
if (currentUser) {
  function test() {
    console.log('Nope.');
  }
}

// good
let test;
if (currentUser) {
  test = () =&gt; {
    console.log('Yup.');
  };
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">currentUser</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">test</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Nope.'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">test</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
