<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">currentUser</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">test</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Yup.'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--arguments-shadow"></a><a name="user-content-7.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--arguments-shadow">7.5</a> Never name a parameter <code>arguments</code>. This will take precedence over the <code>arguments</code> object that is given to every function scope.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function foo(name, options, arguments) {
  // ...
}

// good
function foo(name, options, args) {
  // ...
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">options</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">arguments</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">options</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">args</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-es6-rest"></a><a name="user-content-7.6"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#es6-rest">7.6</a> Never use <code>arguments</code>, opt to use rest syntax <code>...</code> instead. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-rest-params" rel="nofollow"><code>prefer-rest-params</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? <code>...</code> is explicit about which arguments you want pulled. Plus, rest arguments are a real Array, and not merely Array-like like <code>arguments</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function concatenateAll() {
  const args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
  return args.join('');
}

// good
function concatenateAll(...args) {
  return args.join('');
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">concatenateAll</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">args</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Array</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">slice</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">arguments</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">args</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">join</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">''</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">concatenateAll</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>...<span class="pl-s1">args</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">args</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">join</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">''</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-es6-default-parameters"></a><a name="user-content-7.7"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#es6-default-parameters">7.7</a> Use default parameter syntax rather than mutating function arguments.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// really bad
function handleThings(opts) {
  // No! We shouldn’t mutate function arguments.
  // Double bad: if opts is falsy it'll be set to an object which may
  // be what you want but it can introduce subtle bugs.
  opts = opts || {};
  // ...
}

// still bad
function handleThings(opts) {
  if (opts === void 0) {
    opts = {};
  }
  // ...
}

// good
function handleThings(opts = {}) {
  // ...
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// really bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">handleThings</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">opts</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// No! We shouldn’t mutate function arguments.</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Double bad: if opts is falsy it'll be set to an object which may</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// be what you want but it can introduce subtle bugs.</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">opts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">opts</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// still bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">handleThings</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">opts</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">opts</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">opts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">handleThings</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">opts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--default-side-effects"></a><a name="user-content-7.8"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--default-side-effects">7.8</a> Avoid side effects with default parameters.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? They are confusing to reason about.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="var b = 1;
// bad
function count(a = b++) {
  console.log(a);
}
count();  // 1
count();  // 2
count(3); // 3
count();  // 3
"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">count</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-en">count</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>  <span class="pl-c">// 1</span>
<span class="pl-en">count</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>  <span class="pl-c">// 2</span>
<span class="pl-en">count</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// 3</span>
<span class="pl-en">count</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>  <span class="pl-c">// 3</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--defaults-last"></a><a name="user-content-7.9"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--defaults-last">7.9</a> Always put default parameters last. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/default-param-last" rel="nofollow"><code>default-param-last</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function handleThings(opts = {}, name) {
  // ...
}

// good
function handleThings(name, opts = {}) {
  // ...
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">handleThings</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">opts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">handleThings</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">opts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--constructor"></a><a name="user-content-7.10"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--constructor">7.10</a> Never use the Function constructor to create a new function. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-new-func" rel="nofollow"><code>no-new-func</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Creating a function in this way evaluates a string similarly to <code>eval()</code>, which opens vulnerabilities.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
var add = new Function('a', 'b', 'return a + b');

// still bad
var subtract = Function('a', 'b', 'return a - b');
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">add</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Function</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'a'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'b'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'return a + b'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// still bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">subtract</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Function</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'a'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'b'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'return a - b'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--signature-spacing"></a><a name="user-content-7.11"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--signature-spacing">7.11</a> Spacing in a function signature. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/space-before-function-paren" rel="nofollow"><code>space-before-function-paren</code></a> <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/space-before-blocks" rel="nofollow"><code>space-before-blocks</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Consistency is good, and you shouldn’t have to add or remove a space when adding or removing a name.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const f = function(){};
const g = function (){};
const h = function() {};

// good
const x = function () {};
const y = function a() {};
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">f</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">g</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">h</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">a</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--mutate-params"></a><a name="user-content-7.12"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--mutate-params">7.12</a> Never mutate parameters. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-param-reassign.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-param-reassign</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Manipulating objects passed in as parameters can cause unwanted variable side effects in the original caller.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function f1(obj) {
  obj.key = 1;
}

// good
function f2(obj) {
  const key = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, 'key') ? obj.key : 1;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">f1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">key</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">f2</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">key</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">hasOwnProperty</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'key'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> ? <span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">key</span> : <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--reassign-params"></a><a name="user-content-7.13"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--reassign-params">7.13</a> Never reassign parameters. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-param-reassign.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-param-reassign</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Reassigning parameters can lead to unexpected behavior, especially when accessing the <code>arguments</code> object. It can also cause optimization issues, especially in V8.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function f1(a) {
  a = 1;
  // ...
}

function f2(a) {
  if (!a) { a = 1; }
  // ...
}

// good
function f3(a) {
  const b = a || 1;
  // ...
}

function f4(a = 1) {
  // ...
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">f1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">f2</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">f3</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">f4</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--spread-vs-apply"></a><a name="user-content-7.14"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--spread-vs-apply">7.14</a> Prefer the use of the spread syntax <code>...</code> to call variadic functions. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-spread" rel="nofollow"><code>prefer-spread</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? It’s cleaner, you don’t need to supply a context, and you can not easily compose <code>new</code> with <code>apply</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const x = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
console.log.apply(console, x);

// good
const x = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
console.log(...x);

// bad
new (Function.prototype.bind.apply(Date, [null, 2016, 8, 5]));

// good
new Date(...[2016, 8, 5]);
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">log</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">apply</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>...<span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">Function</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bind</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">apply</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">Date</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2016</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">8</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Date</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>...<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">2016</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">8</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-functions--signature-invocation-indentation"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#functions--signature-invocation-indentation">7.15</a> Functions with multiline signatures, or invocations, should be indented just like every other multiline list in this guide: with each item on a line by itself, with a trailing comma on the last item. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/function-paren-newline" rel="nofollow"><code>function-paren-newline</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function foo(bar,
             baz,
             quux) {
  // ...
}

// good
function foo(
  bar,
  baz,
  quux,
) {
  // ...
}

// bad
console.log(foo,
  bar,
  baz);

// good
console.log(
  foo,
  bar,
  baz,
);
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
             <span class="pl-s1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
             <span class="pl-s1">quux</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">quux</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-arrow-functions" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#arrow-functions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Arrow Functions</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-arrows--use-them"></a><a name="user-content-8.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrows--use-them">8.1</a> When you must use an anonymous function (as when passing an inline callback), use arrow function notation. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-arrow-callback.html" rel="nofollow"><code>prefer-arrow-callback</code></a>, <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/arrow-spacing.html" rel="nofollow"><code>arrow-spacing</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? It creates a version of the function that executes in the context of <code>this</code>, which is usually what you want, and is a more concise syntax.</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>Why not? If you have a fairly complicated function, you might move that logic out into its own named function expression.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
[1, 2, 3].map(function (x) {
  const y = x + 1;
  return x * y;
});

// good
[1, 2, 3].map((x) =&gt; {
  const y = x + 1;
  return x * y;
});
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrows--implicit-return"></a><a name="user-content-8.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrows--implicit-return">8.2</a> If the function body consists of a single statement returning an <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Guide/Expressions_and_Operators#Expressions" rel="nofollow">expression</a> without side effects, omit the braces and use the implicit return. Otherwise, keep the braces and use a <code>return</code> statement. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/arrow-parens.html" rel="nofollow"><code>arrow-parens</code></a>, <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/arrow-body-style.html" rel="nofollow"><code>arrow-body-style</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Syntactic sugar. It reads well when multiple functions are chained together.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
[1, 2, 3].map((number) =&gt; {
  const nextNumber = number + 1;
  `A string containing the ${nextNumber}.`;
});

// good
[1, 2, 3].map((number) =&gt; `A string containing the ${number + 1}.`);

// good
[1, 2, 3].map((number) =&gt; {
  const nextNumber = number + 1;
  return `A string containing the ${nextNumber}.`;
});

// good
[1, 2, 3].map((number, index) =&gt; ({
  [index]: number,
}));

// No implicit return with side effects
function foo(callback) {
  const val = callback();
  if (val === true) {
    // Do something if callback returns true
  }
}

let bool = false;

// bad
foo(() =&gt; bool = true);

// good
foo(() =&gt; {
  bool = true;
});
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">number</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">nextNumber</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">number</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-s">`A string containing the <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">nextNumber</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>.`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">number</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s">`A string containing the <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">number</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>.`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">number</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">nextNumber</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">number</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">`A string containing the <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">nextNumber</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>.`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">number</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">index</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">index</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>: <span class="pl-s1">number</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// No implicit return with side effects</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">callback</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">callback</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// Do something if callback returns true</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">bool</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">bool</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">bool</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrows--paren-wrap"></a><a name="user-content-8.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrows--paren-wrap">8.3</a> In case the expression spans over multiple lines, wrap it in parentheses for better readability.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? It shows clearly where the function starts and ends.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
['get', 'post', 'put'].map((httpMethod) =&gt; Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(
    httpMagicObjectWithAVeryLongName,
    httpMethod,
  )
);

// good
['get', 'post', 'put'].map((httpMethod) =&gt; (
  Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(
    httpMagicObjectWithAVeryLongName,
    httpMethod,
  )
));
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'get'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'post'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'put'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">httpMethod</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">hasOwnProperty</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">httpMagicObjectWithAVeryLongName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">httpMethod</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'get'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'post'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'put'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">httpMethod</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">hasOwnProperty</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">httpMagicObjectWithAVeryLongName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">httpMethod</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrows--one-arg-parens"></a><a name="user-content-8.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrows--one-arg-parens">8.4</a> Always include parentheses around arguments for clarity and consistency. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/arrow-parens.html" rel="nofollow"><code>arrow-parens</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Minimizes diff churn when adding or removing arguments.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
[1, 2, 3].map(x =&gt; x * x);

// good
[1, 2, 3].map((x) =&gt; x * x);

// bad
[1, 2, 3].map(number =&gt; (
  `A long string with the ${number}. It’s so long that we don’t want it to take up space on the .map line!`
));

// good
[1, 2, 3].map((number) =&gt; (
  `A long string with the ${number}. It’s so long that we don’t want it to take up space on the .map line!`
));

// bad
[1, 2, 3].map(x =&gt; {
  const y = x + 1;
  return x * y;
});

// good
[1, 2, 3].map((x) =&gt; {
  const y = x + 1;
  return x * y;
});
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">number</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">`A long string with the <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">number</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>. It’s so long that we don’t want it to take up space on the .map line!`</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">number</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s">`A long string with the <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">number</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>. It’s so long that we don’t want it to take up space on the .map line!`</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-arrows--confusing"></a><a name="user-content-8.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#arrows--confusing">8.5</a> Avoid confusing arrow function syntax (<code>=&gt;</code>) with comparison operators (<code>&lt;=</code>, <code>&gt;=</code>). eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-confusing-arrow" rel="nofollow"><code>no-confusing-arrow</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const itemHeight = (item) =&gt; item.height &lt;= 256 ? item.largeSize : item.smallSize;

// bad
const itemHeight = (item) =&gt; item.height &gt;= 256 ? item.largeSize : item.smallSize;

// good
const itemHeight = (item) =&gt; (item.height &lt;= 256 ? item.largeSize : item.smallSize);

// good
const itemHeight = (item) =&gt; {
  const { height, largeSize, smallSize } = item;
  return height &lt;= 256 ? largeSize : smallSize;
};
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">itemHeight</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">256</span> ? <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">largeSize</span> : <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">smallSize</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">itemHeight</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">256</span> ? <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">largeSize</span> : <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">smallSize</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">itemHeight</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">256</span> ? <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">largeSize</span> : <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">smallSize</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">itemHeight</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> height<span class="pl-kos">,</span> largeSize<span class="pl-kos">,</span> smallSize <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">256</span> ? <span class="pl-s1">largeSize</span> : <span class="pl-s1">smallSize</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--implicit-arrow-linebreak"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--implicit-arrow-linebreak">8.6</a> Enforce the location of arrow function bodies with implicit returns. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/implicit-arrow-linebreak" rel="nofollow"><code>implicit-arrow-linebreak</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
(foo) =&gt;
  bar;

(foo) =&gt;
  (bar);

// good
(foo) =&gt; bar;
(foo) =&gt; (bar);
(foo) =&gt; (
   bar
)
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
   <span class="pl-s1">bar</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-classes--constructors" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#classes--constructors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Classes &amp; Constructors</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-constructors--use-class"></a><a name="user-content-9.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#constructors--use-class">9.1</a> Always use <code>class</code>. Avoid manipulating <code>prototype</code> directly.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? <code>class</code> syntax is more concise and easier to reason about.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function Queue(contents = []) {
  this.queue = [...contents];
}
Queue.prototype.pop = function () {
  const value = this.queue[0];
  this.queue.splice(0, 1);
  return value;
};

// good
class Queue {
  constructor(contents = []) {
    this.queue = [...contents];
  }
  pop() {
    const value = this.queue[0];
    this.queue.splice(0, 1);
    return value;
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Queue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">contents</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">queue</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>...<span class="pl-s1">contents</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-v">Queue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">pop</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">queue</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">queue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">splice</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Queue</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">contents</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">queue</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>...<span class="pl-s1">contents</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-en">pop</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">queue</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">queue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">splice</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-constructors--extends"></a><a name="user-content-9.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#constructors--extends">9.2</a> Use <code>extends</code> for inheritance.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? It is a built-in way to inherit prototype functionality without breaking <code>instanceof</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const inherits = require('inherits');
function PeekableQueue(contents) {
  Queue.apply(this, contents);
}
inherits(PeekableQueue, Queue);
PeekableQueue.prototype.peek = function () {
  return this.queue[0];
};

// good
class PeekableQueue extends Queue {
  peek() {
    return this.queue[0];
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">inherits</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'inherits'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">PeekableQueue</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">contents</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Queue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">apply</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">contents</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-s1">inherits</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">PeekableQueue</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-v">Queue</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-v">PeekableQueue</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">peek</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">queue</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">PeekableQueue</span> <span class="pl-k">extends</span> <span class="pl-v">Queue</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">peek</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">queue</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-constructors--chaining"></a><a name="user-content-9.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#constructors--chaining">9.3</a> Methods can return <code>this</code> to help with method chaining.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
Jedi.prototype.jump = function () {
  this.jumping = true;
  return true;
};

Jedi.prototype.setHeight = function (height) {
  this.height = height;
};

const luke = new Jedi();
luke.jump(); // =&gt; true
luke.setHeight(20); // =&gt; undefined

// good
class Jedi {
  jump() {
    this.jumping = true;
    return this;
  }

  setHeight(height) {
    this.height = height;
    return this;
  }
}

const luke = new Jedi();

luke.jump()
  .setHeight(20);
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-v">Jedi</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">jump</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">jumping</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-v">Jedi</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">prototype</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setHeight</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">height</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">height</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">luke</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Jedi</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">luke</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">jump</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; true</span>
<span class="pl-s1">luke</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setHeight</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">20</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; undefined</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Jedi</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">jump</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">jumping</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">setHeight</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">height</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">height</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">luke</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Jedi</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">luke</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">jump</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setHeight</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">20</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-constructors--tostring"></a><a name="user-content-9.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#constructors--tostring">9.4</a> It’s okay to write a custom <code>toString()</code> method, just make sure it works successfully and causes no side effects.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="class Jedi {
  constructor(options = {}) {
    this.name = options.name || 'no name';
  }

  getName() {
    return this.name;
  }

  toString() {
    return `Jedi - ${this.getName()}`;
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Jedi</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">options</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">options</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s">'no name'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">getName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">toString</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">`Jedi - <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">getName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-constructors--no-useless"></a><a name="user-content-9.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#constructors--no-useless">9.5</a> Classes have a default constructor if one is not specified. An empty constructor function or one that just delegates to a parent class is unnecessary. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-useless-constructor" rel="nofollow"><code>no-useless-constructor</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
class Jedi {
  constructor() {}

  getName() {
    return this.name;
  }
}

// bad
class Rey extends Jedi {
  constructor(...args) {
    super(...args);
  }
}

// good
class Rey extends Jedi {
  constructor(...args) {
    super(...args);
    this.name = 'Rey';
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Jedi</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">getName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Rey</span> <span class="pl-k">extends</span> <span class="pl-v">Jedi</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>...<span class="pl-s1">args</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">super</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>...<span class="pl-s1">args</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Rey</span> <span class="pl-k">extends</span> <span class="pl-v">Jedi</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>...<span class="pl-s1">args</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">super</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>...<span class="pl-s1">args</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Rey'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-classes--no-duplicate-members"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#classes--no-duplicate-members">9.6</a> Avoid duplicate class members. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-dupe-class-members" rel="nofollow"><code>no-dupe-class-members</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Duplicate class member declarations will silently prefer the last one - having duplicates is almost certainly a bug.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
class Foo {
  bar() { return 1; }
  bar() { return 2; }
}

// good
class Foo {
  bar() { return 1; }
}

// good
class Foo {
  bar() { return 2; }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-classes--methods-use-this"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#classes--methods-use-this">9.7</a> Class methods should use <code>this</code> or be made into a static method unless an external library or framework requires using specific non-static methods. Being an instance method should indicate that it behaves differently based on properties of the receiver. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/class-methods-use-this" rel="nofollow"><code>class-methods-use-this</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
class Foo {
  bar() {
    console.log('bar');
  }
}

// good - this is used
class Foo {
  bar() {
    console.log(this.bar);
  }
}

// good - constructor is exempt
class Foo {
  constructor() {
    // ...
  }
}

// good - static methods aren't expected to use this
class Foo {
  static bar() {
    console.log('bar');
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'bar'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good - this is used</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good - constructor is exempt</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good - static methods aren't expected to use this</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'bar'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-modules" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#modules"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Modules</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--use-them"></a><a name="user-content-10.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--use-them">10.1</a> Always use modules (<code>import</code>/<code>export</code>) over a non-standard module system. You can always transpile to your preferred module system.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Modules are the future, let’s start using the future now.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const AirbnbStyleGuide = require('./AirbnbStyleGuide');
module.exports = AirbnbStyleGuide.es6;

// ok
import AirbnbStyleGuide from './AirbnbStyleGuide';
export default AirbnbStyleGuide.es6;

// best
import { es6 } from './AirbnbStyleGuide';
export default es6;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">AirbnbStyleGuide</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">require</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-smi">module</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">exports</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">AirbnbStyleGuide</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">es6</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ok</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">AirbnbStyleGuide</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-v">AirbnbStyleGuide</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">es6</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--no-wildcard"></a><a name="user-content-10.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--no-wildcard">10.2</a> Do not use wildcard imports.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? This makes sure you have a single default export.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
import * as AirbnbStyleGuide from './AirbnbStyleGuide';

// good
import AirbnbStyleGuide from './AirbnbStyleGuide';
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-v">AirbnbStyleGuide</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">AirbnbStyleGuide</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--no-export-from-import"></a><a name="user-content-10.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--no-export-from-import">10.3</a> And do not export directly from an import.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Although the one-liner is concise, having one clear way to import and one clear way to export makes things consistent.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
// filename es6.js
export { es6 as default } from './AirbnbStyleGuide';

// good
// filename es6.js
import { es6 } from './AirbnbStyleGuide';
export default es6;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-c">// filename es6.js</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">default</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-c">// filename es6.js</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--no-duplicate-imports"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--no-duplicate-imports">10.4</a> Only import from a path in one place.
eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-duplicate-imports" rel="nofollow"><code>no-duplicate-imports</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Having multiple lines that import from the same path can make code harder to maintain.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
import foo from 'foo';
// … some other imports … //
import { named1, named2 } from 'foo';

// good
import foo, { named1, named2 } from 'foo';

// good
import foo, {
  named1,
  named2,
} from 'foo';
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c">// … some other imports … //</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">named1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">named2</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">named1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">named2</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">named1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">named2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--no-mutable-exports"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--no-mutable-exports">10.5</a> Do not export mutable bindings.
eslint: <a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/no-mutable-exports.md"><code>import/no-mutable-exports</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
