<p>Why? Mutation should be avoided in general, but in particular when exporting mutable bindings. While this technique may be needed for some special cases, in general, only constant references should be exported.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
let foo = 3;
export { foo };

// good
const foo = 3;
export { foo };
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--prefer-default-export"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--prefer-default-export">10.6</a> In modules with a single export, prefer default export over named export.
eslint: <a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/prefer-default-export.md"><code>import/prefer-default-export</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? To encourage more files that only ever export one thing, which is better for readability and maintainability.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
export function foo() {}

// good
export default function foo() {}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--imports-first"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--imports-first">10.7</a> Put all <code>import</code>s above non-import statements.
eslint: <a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/first.md"><code>import/first</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Since <code>import</code>s are hoisted, keeping them all at the top prevents surprising behavior.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
import foo from 'foo';
foo.init();

import bar from 'bar';

// good
import foo from 'foo';
import bar from 'bar';

foo.init();
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">init</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'bar'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'bar'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">init</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--multiline-imports-over-newlines"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--multiline-imports-over-newlines">10.8</a> Multiline imports should be indented just like multiline array and object literals.
eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/object-curly-newline" rel="nofollow"><code>object-curly-newline</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? The curly braces follow the same indentation rules as every other curly brace block in the style guide, as do the trailing commas.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
import {longNameA, longNameB, longNameC, longNameD, longNameE} from 'path';

// good
import {
  longNameA,
  longNameB,
  longNameC,
  longNameD,
  longNameE,
} from 'path';
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">longNameA</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">longNameB</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">longNameC</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">longNameD</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">longNameE</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'path'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">longNameA</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">longNameB</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">longNameC</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">longNameD</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">longNameE</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'path'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--no-webpack-loader-syntax"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--no-webpack-loader-syntax">10.9</a> Disallow Webpack loader syntax in module import statements.
eslint: <a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/no-webpack-loader-syntax.md"><code>import/no-webpack-loader-syntax</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Since using Webpack syntax in the imports couples the code to a module bundler. Prefer using the loader syntax in <code>webpack.config.js</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
import fooSass from 'css!sass!foo.scss';
import barCss from 'style!css!bar.css';

// good
import fooSass from 'foo.scss';
import barCss from 'bar.css';
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">fooSass</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'css!sass!foo.scss'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">barCss</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'style!css!bar.css'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">fooSass</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'foo.scss'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">barCss</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'bar.css'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-modules--import-extensions"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#modules--import-extensions">10.10</a> Do not include JavaScript filename extensions
eslint: <a href="https://github.com/benmosher/eslint-plugin-import/blob/master/docs/rules/extensions.md"><code>import/extensions</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Including extensions inhibits refactoring, and inappropriately hardcodes implementation details of the module you're importing in every consumer.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
import foo from './foo.js';
import bar from './bar.jsx';
import baz from './baz/index.jsx';

// good
import foo from './foo';
import bar from './bar';
import baz from './baz';
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./foo.js'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./bar.jsx'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">baz</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./baz/index.jsx'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./bar'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">baz</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./baz'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-iterators-and-generators" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#iterators-and-generators"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Iterators and Generators</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-iterators--nope"></a><a name="user-content-11.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#iterators--nope">11.1</a> Don’t use iterators. Prefer JavaScript’s higher-order functions instead of loops like <code>for-in</code> or <code>for-of</code>. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-iterator.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-iterator</code></a> <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-restricted-syntax" rel="nofollow"><code>no-restricted-syntax</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? This enforces our immutable rule. Dealing with pure functions that return values is easier to reason about than side effects.</p>
</blockquote>
<blockquote>
<p>Use <code>map()</code> / <code>every()</code> / <code>filter()</code> / <code>find()</code> / <code>findIndex()</code> / <code>reduce()</code> / <code>some()</code> / ... to iterate over arrays, and <code>Object.keys()</code> / <code>Object.values()</code> / <code>Object.entries()</code> to produce arrays so you can iterate over objects.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];

// bad
let sum = 0;
for (let num of numbers) {
  sum += num;
}
sum === 15;

// good
let sum = 0;
numbers.forEach((num) =&gt; {
  sum += num;
});
sum === 15;

// best (use the functional force)
const sum = numbers.reduce((total, num) =&gt; total + num, 0);
sum === 15;

// bad
const increasedByOne = [];
for (let i = 0; i &lt; numbers.length; i++) {
  increasedByOne.push(numbers[i] + 1);
}

// good
const increasedByOne = [];
numbers.forEach((num) =&gt; {
  increasedByOne.push(num + 1);
});

// best (keeping it functional)
const increasedByOne = numbers.map((num) =&gt; num + 1);
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">numbers</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">num</span> <span class="pl-k">of</span> <span class="pl-s1">numbers</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">num</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">15</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">numbers</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">forEach</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">num</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">num</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">15</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best (use the functional force)</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">numbers</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">reduce</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">total</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">num</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">total</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">num</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">15</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">increasedByOne</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">numbers</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">increasedByOne</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">push</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">numbers</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">increasedByOne</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">numbers</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">forEach</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">num</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">increasedByOne</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">push</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">num</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best (keeping it functional)</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">increasedByOne</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">numbers</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">num</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">num</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-generators--nope"></a><a name="user-content-11.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#generators--nope">11.2</a> Don’t use generators for now.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? They don’t transpile well to ES5.</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-generators--spacing"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#generators--spacing">11.3</a> If you must use generators, or if you disregard <a href="#generators--nope">our advice</a>, make sure their function signature is spaced properly. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/generator-star-spacing" rel="nofollow"><code>generator-star-spacing</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? <code>function</code> and <code>*</code> are part of the same conceptual keyword - <code>*</code> is not a modifier for <code>function</code>, <code>function*</code> is a unique construct, different from <code>function</code>.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function * foo() {
  // ...
}

// bad
const bar = function * () {
  // ...
};

// bad
const baz = function *() {
  // ...
};

// bad
const quux = function*() {
  // ...
};

// bad
function*foo() {
  // ...
}

// bad
function *foo() {
  // ...
}

// very bad
function
*
foo() {
  // ...
}

// very bad
const wat = function
*
() {
  // ...
};

// good
function* foo() {
  // ...
}

// good
const foo = function* () {
  // ...
};
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">baz</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">quux</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// very bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span>
<span class="pl-c1">*</span>
<span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// very bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">wat</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span>
<span class="pl-c1">*</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-properties" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#properties"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Properties</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-properties--dot"></a><a name="user-content-12.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#properties--dot">12.1</a> Use dot notation when accessing properties. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/dot-notation.html" rel="nofollow"><code>dot-notation</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const luke = {
  jedi: true,
  age: 28,
};

// bad
const isJedi = luke['jedi'];

// good
const isJedi = luke.jedi;
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">luke</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">jedi</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">age</span>: <span class="pl-c1">28</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">isJedi</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">luke</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'jedi'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">isJedi</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">luke</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">jedi</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-properties--bracket"></a><a name="user-content-12.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#properties--bracket">12.2</a> Use bracket notation <code>[]</code> when accessing properties with a variable.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const luke = {
  jedi: true,
  age: 28,
};

function getProp(prop) {
  return luke[prop];
}

const isJedi = getProp('jedi');
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">luke</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">jedi</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">age</span>: <span class="pl-c1">28</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getProp</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">prop</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">luke</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">prop</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">isJedi</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getProp</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'jedi'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-es2016-properties--exponentiation-operator"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#es2016-properties--exponentiation-operator">12.3</a> Use exponentiation operator <code>**</code> when calculating exponentiations. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-restricted-properties" rel="nofollow"><code>no-restricted-properties</code></a>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const binary = Math.pow(2, 10);

// good
const binary = 2 ** 10;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">binary</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">pow</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">binary</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-variables" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Variables</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-variables--const"></a><a name="user-content-13.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#variables--const">13.1</a> Always use <code>const</code> or <code>let</code> to declare variables. Not doing so will result in global variables. We want to avoid polluting the global namespace. Captain Planet warned us of that. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-undef" rel="nofollow"><code>no-undef</code></a> <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-const" rel="nofollow"><code>prefer-const</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
superPower = new SuperPower();

// good
const superPower = new SuperPower();
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-s1">superPower</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">SuperPower</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">superPower</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">SuperPower</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-variables--one-const"></a><a name="user-content-13.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#variables--one-const">13.2</a> Use one <code>const</code> or <code>let</code> declaration per variable or assignment. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/one-var.html" rel="nofollow"><code>one-var</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? It’s easier to add new variable declarations this way, and you never have to worry about swapping out a <code>;</code> for a <code>,</code> or introducing punctuation-only diffs. You can also step through each declaration with the debugger, instead of jumping through all of them at once.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const items = getItems(),
    goSportsTeam = true,
    dragonball = 'z';

// bad
// (compare to above, and try to spot the mistake)
const items = getItems(),
    goSportsTeam = true;
    dragonball = 'z';

// good
const items = getItems();
const goSportsTeam = true;
const dragonball = 'z';
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">items</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getItems</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">goSportsTeam</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">dragonball</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'z'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-c">// (compare to above, and try to spot the mistake)</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">items</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getItems</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">goSportsTeam</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">dragonball</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'z'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">items</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getItems</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">goSportsTeam</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">dragonball</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'z'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-variables--const-let-group"></a><a name="user-content-13.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#variables--const-let-group">13.3</a> Group all your <code>const</code>s and then group all your <code>let</code>s.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? This is helpful when later on you might need to assign a variable depending on one of the previously assigned variables.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
let i, len, dragonball,
    items = getItems(),
    goSportsTeam = true;

// bad
let i;
const items = getItems();
let dragonball;
const goSportsTeam = true;
let len;

// good
const goSportsTeam = true;
const items = getItems();
let dragonball;
let i;
let length;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">len</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">dragonball</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">items</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getItems</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">goSportsTeam</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">items</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getItems</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">dragonball</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">goSportsTeam</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">len</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">goSportsTeam</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">items</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getItems</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">dragonball</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-variables--define-where-used"></a><a name="user-content-13.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#variables--define-where-used">13.4</a> Assign variables where you need them, but place them in a reasonable place.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? <code>let</code> and <code>const</code> are block scoped and not function scoped.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad - unnecessary function call
function checkName(hasName) {
  const name = getName();

  if (hasName === 'test') {
    return false;
  }

  if (name === 'test') {
    this.setName('');
    return false;
  }

  return name;
}

// good
function checkName(hasName) {
  if (hasName === 'test') {
    return false;
  }

  const name = getName();

  if (name === 'test') {
    this.setName('');
    return false;
  }

  return name;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad - unnecessary function call</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">checkName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">hasName</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">hasName</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'test'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'test'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">''</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">checkName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">hasName</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">hasName</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'test'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'test'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">''</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-variables--no-chain-assignment"></a><a name="user-content-13.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#variables--no-chain-assignment">13.5</a> Don’t chain variable assignments. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-multi-assign" rel="nofollow"><code>no-multi-assign</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Chaining variable assignments creates implicit global variables.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
(function example() {
  // JavaScript interprets this as
  // let a = ( b = ( c = 1 ) );
  // The let keyword only applies to variable a; variables b and c become
  // global variables.
  let a = b = c = 1;
}());

console.log(a); // throws ReferenceError
console.log(b); // 1
console.log(c); // 1

// good
(function example() {
  let a = 1;
  let b = a;
  let c = a;
}());

console.log(a); // throws ReferenceError
console.log(b); // throws ReferenceError
console.log(c); // throws ReferenceError

// the same applies for `const`
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// JavaScript interprets this as</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// let a = ( b = ( c = 1 ) );</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// The let keyword only applies to variable a; variables b and c become</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// global variables.</span>
  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// throws ReferenceError</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// 1</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// 1</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// throws ReferenceError</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// throws ReferenceError</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// throws ReferenceError</span>

<span class="pl-c">// the same applies for `const`</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-variables--unary-increment-decrement"></a><a name="user-content-13.6"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#variables--unary-increment-decrement">13.6</a> Avoid using unary increments and decrements (<code>++</code>, <code>--</code>). eslint <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-plusplus" rel="nofollow"><code>no-plusplus</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Per the eslint documentation, unary increment and decrement statements are subject to automatic semicolon insertion and can cause silent errors with incrementing or decrementing values within an application. It is also more expressive to mutate your values with statements like <code>num += 1</code> instead of <code>num++</code> or <code>num ++</code>. Disallowing unary increment and decrement statements also prevents you from pre-incrementing/pre-decrementing values unintentionally which can also cause unexpected behavior in your programs.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad

const array = [1, 2, 3];
let num = 1;
num++;
--num;

let sum = 0;
let truthyCount = 0;
for (let i = 0; i &lt; array.length; i++) {
  let value = array[i];
  sum += value;
  if (value) {
    truthyCount++;
  }
}

// good

const array = [1, 2, 3];
let num = 1;
num += 1;
num -= 1;

const sum = array.reduce((a, b) =&gt; a + b, 0);
const truthyCount = array.filter(Boolean).length;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">array</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">num</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">num</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c1">--</span><span class="pl-s1">num</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">truthyCount</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">array</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">array</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">truthyCount</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">array</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">num</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">num</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">num</span> <span class="pl-c1">-=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">sum</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">array</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">reduce</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">truthyCount</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">array</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">filter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">Boolean</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-variables--linebreak"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#variables--linebreak">13.7</a> Avoid linebreaks before or after <code>=</code> in an assignment. If your assignment violates <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/max-len.html" rel="nofollow"><code>max-len</code></a>, surround the value in parens. eslint <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/operator-linebreak.html" rel="nofollow"><code>operator-linebreak</code></a>.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Linebreaks surrounding <code>=</code> can obfuscate the value of an assignment.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const foo =
  superLongLongLongLongLongLongLongLongFunctionName();

// bad
const foo
  = 'superLongLongLongLongLongLongLongLongString';

// good
const foo = (
  superLongLongLongLongLongLongLongLongFunctionName()
);

// good
const foo = 'superLongLongLongLongLongLongLongLongString';
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span>
  <span class="pl-en">superLongLongLongLongLongLongLongLongFunctionName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'superLongLongLongLongLongLongLongLongString'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-en">superLongLongLongLongLongLongLongLongFunctionName</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'superLongLongLongLongLongLongLongLongString'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-variables--no-unused-vars"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#variables--no-unused-vars">13.8</a> Disallow unused variables. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unused-vars" rel="nofollow"><code>no-unused-vars</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Variables that are declared and not used anywhere in the code are most likely an error due to incomplete refactoring. Such variables take up space in the code and can lead to confusion by readers.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad

var some_unused_var = 42;

// Write-only variables are not considered as used.
var y = 10;
y = 5;

// A read for a modification of itself is not considered as used.
var z = 0;
z = z + 1;

// Unused function arguments.
function getX(x, y) {
    return x;
}

// good

function getXPlusY(x, y) {
  return x + y;
}

var x = 1;
var y = a + 2;

alert(getXPlusY(x, y));

// 'type' is ignored even if unused because it has a rest property sibling.
// This is a form of extracting an object that omits the specified keys.
var { type, ...coords } = data;
// 'coords' is now the 'data' object without its 'type' property.
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">some_unused_var</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">42</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Write-only variables are not considered as used.</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// A read for a modification of itself is not considered as used.</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">z</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">z</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">z</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Unused function arguments.</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getX</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getXPlusY</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-en">alert</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-en">getXPlusY</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// 'type' is ignored even if unused because it has a rest property sibling.</span>
<span class="pl-c">// This is a form of extracting an object that omits the specified keys.</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> type<span class="pl-kos">,</span> ...<span class="pl-s1">coords</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-c">// 'coords' is now the 'data' object without its 'type' property.</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-hoisting" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#hoisting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Hoisting</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-hoisting--about"></a><a name="user-content-14.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#hoisting--about">14.1</a> <code>var</code> declarations get hoisted to the top of their closest enclosing function scope, their assignment does not. <code>const</code> and <code>let</code> declarations are blessed with a new concept called <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/let#Temporal_dead_zone" rel="nofollow">Temporal Dead Zones (TDZ)</a>. It’s important to know why <a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200121061528/http://es-discourse.com/t/why-typeof-is-no-longer-safe/15" rel="nofollow">typeof is no longer safe</a>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// we know this wouldn’t work (assuming there
// is no notDefined global variable)
function example() {
  console.log(notDefined); // =&gt; throws a ReferenceError
}

// creating a variable declaration after you
// reference the variable will work due to
// variable hoisting. Note: the assignment
// value of `true` is not hoisted.
function example() {
  console.log(declaredButNotAssigned); // =&gt; undefined
  var declaredButNotAssigned = true;
}

// the interpreter is hoisting the variable
// declaration to the top of the scope,
// which means our example could be rewritten as:
function example() {
  let declaredButNotAssigned;
  console.log(declaredButNotAssigned); // =&gt; undefined
  declaredButNotAssigned = true;
}

// using const and let
function example() {
  console.log(declaredButNotAssigned); // =&gt; throws a ReferenceError
  console.log(typeof declaredButNotAssigned); // =&gt; throws a ReferenceError
  const declaredButNotAssigned = true;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// we know this wouldn’t work (assuming there</span>
<span class="pl-c">// is no notDefined global variable)</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">notDefined</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; throws a ReferenceError</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// creating a variable declaration after you</span>
<span class="pl-c">// reference the variable will work due to</span>
<span class="pl-c">// variable hoisting. Note: the assignment</span>
<span class="pl-c">// value of `true` is not hoisted.</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">declaredButNotAssigned</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; undefined</span>
  <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">declaredButNotAssigned</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// the interpreter is hoisting the variable</span>
<span class="pl-c">// declaration to the top of the scope,</span>
<span class="pl-c">// which means our example could be rewritten as:</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">declaredButNotAssigned</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">declaredButNotAssigned</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; undefined</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">declaredButNotAssigned</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// using const and let</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">declaredButNotAssigned</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; throws a ReferenceError</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">typeof</span> <span class="pl-s1">declaredButNotAssigned</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; throws a ReferenceError</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">declaredButNotAssigned</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-hoisting--anon-expressions"></a><a name="user-content-14.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#hoisting--anon-expressions">14.2</a> Anonymous function expressions hoist their variable name, but not the function assignment.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="function example() {
  console.log(anonymous); // =&gt; undefined

  anonymous(); // =&gt; TypeError anonymous is not a function

  var anonymous = function () {
    console.log('anonymous function expression');
  };
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">anonymous</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; undefined</span>

  <span class="pl-en">anonymous</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; TypeError anonymous is not a function</span>

  <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">anonymous</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'anonymous function expression'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-hoisting--named-expresions"></a><a name="user-content-hoisting--named-expressions"></a><a name="user-content-14.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#hoisting--named-expressions">14.3</a> Named function expressions hoist the variable name, not the function name or the function body.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="function example() {
  console.log(named); // =&gt; undefined

  named(); // =&gt; TypeError named is not a function

  superPower(); // =&gt; ReferenceError superPower is not defined

  var named = function superPower() {
    console.log('Flying');
  };
}

// the same is true when the function name
// is the same as the variable name.
function example() {
  console.log(named); // =&gt; undefined

  named(); // =&gt; TypeError named is not a function

  var named = function named() {
    console.log('named');
  };
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">named</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; undefined</span>

  <span class="pl-en">named</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; TypeError named is not a function</span>

  <span class="pl-en">superPower</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; ReferenceError superPower is not defined</span>

  <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">named</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">superPower</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Flying'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// the same is true when the function name</span>
<span class="pl-c">// is the same as the variable name.</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">named</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; undefined</span>

  <span class="pl-en">named</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; TypeError named is not a function</span>

  <span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">named</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">named</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'named'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-hoisting--declarations"></a><a name="user-content-14.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#hoisting--declarations">14.4</a> Function declarations hoist their name and the function body.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="function example() {
  superPower(); // =&gt; Flying

  function superPower() {
    console.log('Flying');
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">example</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">superPower</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; Flying</span>

  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">superPower</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Flying'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>For more information refer to <a href="http://www.adequatelygood.com/2010/2/JavaScript-Scoping-and-Hoisting/" rel="nofollow">JavaScript Scoping &amp; Hoisting</a> by <a href="http://www.adequatelygood.com/" rel="nofollow">Ben Cherry</a>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-comparison-operators--equality" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#comparison-operators--equality"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Comparison Operators &amp; Equality</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-comparison--eqeqeq"></a><a name="user-content-15.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#comparison--eqeqeq">15.1</a> Use <code>===</code> and <code>!==</code> over <code>==</code> and <code>!=</code>. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/eqeqeq.html" rel="nofollow"><code>eqeqeq</code></a></li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comparison--if"></a><a name="user-content-15.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comparison--if">15.2</a> Conditional statements such as the <code>if</code> statement evaluate their expression using coercion with the <code>ToBoolean</code> abstract method and always follow these simple rules:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Objects</strong> evaluate to <strong>true</strong></li>
<li><strong>Undefined</strong> evaluates to <strong>false</strong></li>
<li><strong>Null</strong> evaluates to <strong>false</strong></li>
<li><strong>Booleans</strong> evaluate to <strong>the value of the boolean</strong></li>
<li><strong>Numbers</strong> evaluate to <strong>false</strong> if <strong>+0, -0, or NaN</strong>, otherwise <strong>true</strong></li>
<li><strong>Strings</strong> evaluate to <strong>false</strong> if an empty string <code>''</code>, otherwise <strong>true</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="if ([0] &amp;&amp; []) {
  // true
  // an array (even an empty one) is an object, objects will evaluate to true
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// true</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// an array (even an empty one) is an object, objects will evaluate to true</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comparison--shortcuts"></a><a name="user-content-15.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comparison--shortcuts">15.3</a> Use shortcuts for booleans, but explicit comparisons for strings and numbers.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
if (isValid === true) {
  // ...
}

// good
if (isValid) {
  // ...
}

// bad
if (name) {
  // ...
}

// good
if (name !== '') {
  // ...
}

// bad
if (collection.length) {
  // ...
}

// good
if (collection.length &gt; 0) {
  // ...
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">isValid</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">isValid</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">!==</span> <span class="pl-s">''</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">collection</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">collection</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comparison--moreinfo"></a><a name="user-content-15.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#comparison--moreinfo">15.4</a> For more information see <a href="https://javascriptweblog.wordpress.com/2011/02/07/truth-equality-and-javascript/#more-2108" rel="nofollow">Truth Equality and JavaScript</a> by Angus Croll.</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comparison--switch-blocks"></a><a name="user-content-15.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comparison--switch-blocks">15.5</a> Use braces to create blocks in <code>case</code> and <code>default</code> clauses that contain lexical declarations (e.g. <code>let</code>, <code>const</code>, <code>function</code>, and <code>class</code>). eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-case-declarations.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-case-declarations</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Lexical declarations are visible in the entire <code>switch</code> block but only get initialized when assigned, which only happens when its <code>case</code> is reached. This causes problems when multiple <code>case</code> clauses attempt to define the same thing.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
switch (foo) {
  case 1:
    let x = 1;
    break;
  case 2:
    const y = 2;
    break;
  case 3:
    function f() {
      // ...
    }
    break;
  default:
    class C {}
}

// good
switch (foo) {
  case 1: {
    let x = 1;
    break;
  }
  case 2: {
    const y = 2;
    break;
  }
  case 3: {
    function f() {
      // ...
    }
    break;
  }
  case 4:
    bar();
    break;
  default: {
    class C {}
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">switch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">f</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">default</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">C</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">switch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">f</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">4</span>:
    <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">default</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">C</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comparison--nested-ternaries"></a><a name="user-content-15.6"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comparison--nested-ternaries">15.6</a> Ternaries should not be nested and generally be single line expressions. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-nested-ternary.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-nested-ternary</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const foo = maybe1 &gt; maybe2
  ? &quot;bar&quot;
  : value1 &gt; value2 ? &quot;baz&quot; : null;

// split into 2 separated ternary expressions
const maybeNull = value1 &gt; value2 ? 'baz' : null;

// better
const foo = maybe1 &gt; maybe2
  ? 'bar'
  : maybeNull;

// best
const foo = maybe1 &gt; maybe2 ? 'bar' : maybeNull;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">maybe1</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">maybe2</span>
  ? <span class="pl-s">"bar"</span>
  : <span class="pl-s1">value1</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">value2</span> ? <span class="pl-s">"baz"</span> : <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// split into 2 separated ternary expressions</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">maybeNull</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">value1</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">value2</span> ? <span class="pl-s">'baz'</span> : <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// better</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">maybe1</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">maybe2</span>
  ? <span class="pl-s">'bar'</span>
  : <span class="pl-s1">maybeNull</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best</span>
