<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">maybe1</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">maybe2</span> ? <span class="pl-s">'bar'</span> : <span class="pl-s1">maybeNull</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comparison--unneeded-ternary"></a><a name="user-content-15.7"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comparison--unneeded-ternary">15.7</a> Avoid unneeded ternary statements. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unneeded-ternary.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-unneeded-ternary</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const foo = a ? a : b;
const bar = c ? true : false;
const baz = c ? false : true;

// good
const foo = a || b;
const bar = !!c;
const baz = !c;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> ? <span class="pl-s1">a</span> : <span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> ? <span class="pl-c1">true</span> : <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">baz</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> ? <span class="pl-c1">false</span> : <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">baz</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comparison--no-mixed-operators"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comparison--no-mixed-operators">15.8</a> When mixing operators, enclose them in parentheses. The only exception is the standard arithmetic operators: <code>+</code>, <code>-</code>, and <code>**</code> since their precedence is broadly understood. We recommend enclosing <code>/</code> and <code>*</code> in parentheses because their precedence can be ambiguous when they are mixed.
eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-mixed-operators.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-mixed-operators</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? This improves readability and clarifies the developer’s intention.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const foo = a &amp;&amp; b &lt; 0 || c &gt; 0 || d + 1 === 0;

// bad
const bar = a ** b - 5 % d;

// bad
// one may be confused into thinking (a || b) &amp;&amp; c
if (a || b &amp;&amp; c) {
  return d;
}

// bad
const bar = a + b / c * d;

// good
const foo = (a &amp;&amp; b &lt; 0) || c &gt; 0 || (d + 1 === 0);

// good
const bar = a ** b - (5 % d);

// good
if (a || (b &amp;&amp; c)) {
  return d;
}

// good
const bar = a + (b / c) * d;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">d</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span> <span class="pl-c1">%</span> <span class="pl-s1">d</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-c">// one may be confused into thinking (a || b) &amp;&amp; c</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">d</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">d</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">d</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">**</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">5</span> <span class="pl-c1">%</span> <span class="pl-s1">d</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">d</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">d</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-blocks" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#blocks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Blocks</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-blocks--braces"></a><a name="user-content-16.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#blocks--braces">16.1</a> Use braces with all multiline blocks. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/nonblock-statement-body-position" rel="nofollow"><code>nonblock-statement-body-position</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
if (test)
  return false;

// good
if (test) return false;

// good
if (test) {
  return false;
}

// bad
function foo() { return false; }

// good
function bar() {
  return false;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">test</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">test</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">test</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-blocks--cuddled-elses"></a><a name="user-content-16.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#blocks--cuddled-elses">16.2</a> If you’re using multiline blocks with <code>if</code> and <code>else</code>, put <code>else</code> on the same line as your <code>if</code> block’s closing brace. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/brace-style.html" rel="nofollow"><code>brace-style</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
if (test) {
  thing1();
  thing2();
}
else {
  thing3();
}

// good
if (test) {
  thing1();
  thing2();
} else {
  thing3();
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">test</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing2</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing3</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">test</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing2</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing3</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-blocks--no-else-return"></a><a name="user-content-16.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#blocks--no-else-return">16.3</a> If an <code>if</code> block always executes a <code>return</code> statement, the subsequent <code>else</code> block is unnecessary. A <code>return</code> in an <code>else if</code> block following an <code>if</code> block that contains a <code>return</code> can be separated into multiple <code>if</code> blocks. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-else-return" rel="nofollow"><code>no-else-return</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function foo() {
  if (x) {
    return x;
  } else {
    return y;
  }
}

// bad
function cats() {
  if (x) {
    return x;
  } else if (y) {
    return y;
  }
}

// bad
function dogs() {
  if (x) {
    return x;
  } else {
    if (y) {
      return y;
    }
  }
}

// good
function foo() {
  if (x) {
    return x;
  }

  return y;
}

// good
function cats() {
  if (x) {
    return x;
  }

  if (y) {
    return y;
  }
}

// good
function dogs(x) {
  if (x) {
    if (z) {
      return y;
    }
  } else {
    return z;
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">cats</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">dogs</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">cats</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">dogs</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">z</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-control-statements" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#control-statements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Control Statements</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-control-statements"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#control-statements">17.1</a> In case your control statement (<code>if</code>, <code>while</code> etc.) gets too long or exceeds the maximum line length, each (grouped) condition could be put into a new line. The logical operator should begin the line.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Requiring operators at the beginning of the line keeps the operators aligned and follows a pattern similar to method chaining. This also improves readability by making it easier to visually follow complex logic.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
if ((foo === 123 || bar === 'abc') &amp;&amp; doesItLookGoodWhenItBecomesThatLong() &amp;&amp; isThisReallyHappening()) {
  thing1();
}

// bad
if (foo === 123 &amp;&amp;
  bar === 'abc') {
  thing1();
}

// bad
if (foo === 123
  &amp;&amp; bar === 'abc') {
  thing1();
}

// bad
if (
  foo === 123 &amp;&amp;
  bar === 'abc'
) {
  thing1();
}

// good
if (
  foo === 123
  &amp;&amp; bar === 'abc'
) {
  thing1();
}

// good
if (
  (foo === 123 || bar === 'abc')
  &amp;&amp; doesItLookGoodWhenItBecomesThatLong()
  &amp;&amp; isThisReallyHappening()
) {
  thing1();
}

// good
if (foo === 123 &amp;&amp; bar === 'abc') {
  thing1();
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">123</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'abc'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-en">doesItLookGoodWhenItBecomesThatLong</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-en">isThisReallyHappening</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">123</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'abc'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">123</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'abc'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">123</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'abc'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">123</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'abc'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">123</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'abc'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-en">doesItLookGoodWhenItBecomesThatLong</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-en">isThisReallyHappening</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-c1">123</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">'abc'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">thing1</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-control-statement--value-selection"></a><a name="user-content-control-statements--value-selection"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#control-statements--value-selection">17.2</a> Don't use selection operators in place of control statements.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
!isRunning &amp;&amp; startRunning();

// good
if (!isRunning) {
  startRunning();
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">isRunning</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-en">startRunning</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">isRunning</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">startRunning</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-comments" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#comments"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Comments</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-comments--multiline"></a><a name="user-content-17.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comments--multiline">18.1</a> Use <code>/** ... */</code> for multiline comments.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
// make() returns a new element
// based on the passed in tag name
//
// @param {String} tag
// @return {Element} element
function make(tag) {

  // ...

  return element;
}

// good
/**
 * make() returns a new element
 * based on the passed-in tag name
 */
function make(tag) {

  // ...

  return element;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-c">// make() returns a new element</span>
<span class="pl-c">// based on the passed in tag name</span>
<span class="pl-c">//</span>
<span class="pl-c">// <span class="pl-k">@param</span> {<span class="pl-smi">String</span>} tag</span>
<span class="pl-c">// <span class="pl-k">@return</span> {<span class="pl-smi">Element</span>} element</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">make</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">tag</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">element</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c"> * make() returns a new element</span>
<span class="pl-c"> * based on the passed-in tag name</span>
<span class="pl-c"> */</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">make</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">tag</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">element</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comments--singleline"></a><a name="user-content-17.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comments--singleline">18.2</a> Use <code>//</code> for single line comments. Place single line comments on a newline above the subject of the comment. Put an empty line before the comment unless it’s on the first line of a block.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const active = true;  // is current tab

// good
// is current tab
const active = true;

// bad
function getType() {
  console.log('fetching type...');
  // set the default type to 'no type'
  const type = this.type || 'no type';

  return type;
}

// good
function getType() {
  console.log('fetching type...');

  // set the default type to 'no type'
  const type = this.type || 'no type';

  return type;
}

// also good
function getType() {
  // set the default type to 'no type'
  const type = this.type || 'no type';

  return type;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">active</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>  <span class="pl-c">// is current tab</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-c">// is current tab</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">active</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getType</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'fetching type...'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// set the default type to 'no type'</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">type</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">type</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s">'no type'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getType</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'fetching type...'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// set the default type to 'no type'</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">type</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">type</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s">'no type'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// also good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">getType</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// set the default type to 'no type'</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">type</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">type</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s">'no type'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comments--spaces"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comments--spaces">18.3</a> Start all comments with a space to make it easier to read. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/spaced-comment" rel="nofollow"><code>spaced-comment</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
//is current tab
const active = true;

// good
// is current tab
const active = true;

// bad
/**
 *make() returns a new element
 *based on the passed-in tag name
 */
function make(tag) {

  // ...

  return element;
}

// good
/**
 * make() returns a new element
 * based on the passed-in tag name
 */
function make(tag) {

  // ...

  return element;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-c">//is current tab</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">active</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-c">// is current tab</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">active</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c"> *make() returns a new element</span>
<span class="pl-c"> *based on the passed-in tag name</span>
<span class="pl-c"> */</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">make</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">tag</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">element</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c"> * make() returns a new element</span>
<span class="pl-c"> * based on the passed-in tag name</span>
<span class="pl-c"> */</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">make</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">tag</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">element</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comments--actionitems"></a><a name="user-content-17.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#comments--actionitems">18.4</a> Prefixing your comments with <code>FIXME</code> or <code>TODO</code> helps other developers quickly understand if you’re pointing out a problem that needs to be revisited, or if you’re suggesting a solution to the problem that needs to be implemented. These are different than regular comments because they are actionable. The actions are <code>FIXME: -- need to figure this out</code> or <code>TODO: -- need to implement</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comments--fixme"></a><a name="user-content-17.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comments--fixme">18.5</a> Use <code>// FIXME:</code> to annotate problems.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="class Calculator extends Abacus {
  constructor() {
    super();

    // FIXME: shouldn’t use a global here
    total = 0;
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Calculator</span> <span class="pl-k">extends</span> <span class="pl-v">Abacus</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">super</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

    <span class="pl-c">// FIXME: shouldn’t use a global here</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">total</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-comments--todo"></a><a name="user-content-17.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#comments--todo">18.6</a> Use <code>// TODO:</code> to annotate solutions to problems.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="class Calculator extends Abacus {
  constructor() {
    super();

    // TODO: total should be configurable by an options param
    this.total = 0;
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Calculator</span> <span class="pl-k">extends</span> <span class="pl-v">Abacus</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">super</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

    <span class="pl-c">// TODO: total should be configurable by an options param</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">total</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-whitespace" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#whitespace"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Whitespace</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--spaces"></a><a name="user-content-18.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--spaces">19.1</a> Use soft tabs (space character) set to 2 spaces. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/indent.html" rel="nofollow"><code>indent</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function foo() {
∙∙∙∙let name;
}

// bad
function bar() {
∙let name;
}

// good
function baz() {
∙∙let name;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-s1">∙∙∙∙let</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-s1">∙let</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
<span class="pl-s1">∙∙let</span> <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--before-blocks"></a><a name="user-content-18.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--before-blocks">19.2</a> Place 1 space before the leading brace. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/space-before-blocks.html" rel="nofollow"><code>space-before-blocks</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function test(){
  console.log('test');
}

// good
function test() {
  console.log('test');
}

// bad
dog.set('attr',{
  age: '1 year',
  breed: 'Bernese Mountain Dog',
});

// good
dog.set('attr', {
  age: '1 year',
  breed: 'Bernese Mountain Dog',
});
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">test</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'test'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">test</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'test'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-s1">dog</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">set</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'attr'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">age</span>: <span class="pl-s">'1 year'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">breed</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Bernese Mountain Dog'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-s1">dog</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">set</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'attr'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">age</span>: <span class="pl-s">'1 year'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">breed</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Bernese Mountain Dog'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--around-keywords"></a><a name="user-content-18.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--around-keywords">19.3</a> Place 1 space before the opening parenthesis in control statements (<code>if</code>, <code>while</code> etc.). Place no space between the argument list and the function name in function calls and declarations. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/keyword-spacing.html" rel="nofollow"><code>keyword-spacing</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
if(isJedi) {
  fight ();
}

// good
if (isJedi) {
  fight();
}

// bad
function fight () {
  console.log ('Swooosh!');
}

// good
function fight() {
  console.log('Swooosh!');
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">isJedi</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">fight</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">isJedi</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">fight</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">fight</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Swooosh!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">fight</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Swooosh!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--infix-ops"></a><a name="user-content-18.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--infix-ops">19.4</a> Set off operators with spaces. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/space-infix-ops.html" rel="nofollow"><code>space-infix-ops</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const x=y+5;

// good
const x = y + 5;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-c1">+</span><span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--newline-at-end"></a><a name="user-content-18.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--newline-at-end">19.5</a> End files with a single newline character. eslint: <a href="https://github.com/eslint/eslint/blob/master/docs/rules/eol-last.md"><code>eol-last</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
import { es6 } from './AirbnbStyleGuide';
  // ...
export default es6;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
import { es6 } from './AirbnbStyleGuide';
  // ...
export default es6;↵
↵
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span><span class="pl-s1">↵</span>
<span class="pl-s1">↵</span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// good
import { es6 } from './AirbnbStyleGuide';
  // ...
export default es6;↵
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./AirbnbStyleGuide'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-s1">es6</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span><span class="pl-s1">↵</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--chains"></a><a name="user-content-18.6"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--chains">19.6</a> Use indentation when making long method chains (more than 2 method chains). Use a leading dot, which
emphasizes that the line is a method call, not a new statement. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/newline-per-chained-call" rel="nofollow"><code>newline-per-chained-call</code></a> <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-whitespace-before-property" rel="nofollow"><code>no-whitespace-before-property</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
$('#items').find('.selected').highlight().end().find('.open').updateCount();

// bad
$('#items').
  find('.selected').
    highlight().
    end().
  find('.open').
    updateCount();

// good
$('#items')
  .find('.selected')
    .highlight()
    .end()
  .find('.open')
    .updateCount();

// bad
const leds = stage.selectAll('.led').data(data).enter().append('svg:svg').classed('led', true)
    .attr('width', (radius + margin) * 2).append('svg:g')
    .attr('transform', `translate(${radius + margin},${radius + margin})`)
    .call(tron.led);

// good
const leds = stage.selectAll('.led')
    .data(data)
  .enter().append('svg:svg')
    .classed('led', true)
    .attr('width', (radius + margin) * 2)
  .append('svg:g')
    .attr('transform', `translate(${radius + margin},${radius + margin})`)
    .call(tron.led);

// good
const leds = stage.selectAll('.led').data(data);
const svg = leds.enter().append('svg:svg');
svg.classed('led', true).attr('width', (radius + margin) * 2);
const g = svg.append('svg:g');
g.attr('transform', `translate(${radius + margin},${radius + margin})`).call(tron.led);
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-en">$</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'#items'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">find</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.selected'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">highlight</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">end</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">find</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.open'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">updateCount</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-en">$</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'#items'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span>
  <span class="pl-en">find</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.selected'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span>
    <span class="pl-en">highlight</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span>
    <span class="pl-en">end</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span>
  <span class="pl-en">find</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.open'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span>
    <span class="pl-en">updateCount</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-en">$</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'#items'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">find</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.selected'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">highlight</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">end</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">find</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.open'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">updateCount</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">leds</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">stage</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">selectAll</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.led'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">data</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">enter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">append</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'svg:svg'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">classed</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'led'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">attr</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'width'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">append</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'svg:g'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">attr</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'transform'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">`translate(<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>,<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>)`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">tron</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">led</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">leds</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">stage</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">selectAll</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.led'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">data</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">enter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">append</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'svg:svg'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">classed</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'led'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">attr</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'width'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">append</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'svg:g'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">attr</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'transform'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">`translate(<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>,<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>)`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">tron</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">led</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">leds</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">stage</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">selectAll</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'.led'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">data</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">svg</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">leds</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">enter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">append</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'svg:svg'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">svg</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">classed</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'led'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">attr</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'width'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">g</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">svg</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">append</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'svg:g'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">g</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">attr</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'transform'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">`translate(<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>,<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">margin</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>)`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">call</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">tron</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">led</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--after-blocks"></a><a name="user-content-18.7"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--after-blocks">19.7</a> Leave a blank line after blocks and before the next statement.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
if (foo) {
  return bar;
}
return baz;

// good
if (foo) {
  return bar;
}

return baz;

// bad
const obj = {
  foo() {
  },
  bar() {
  },
};
return obj;

// good
const obj = {
  foo() {
  },

  bar() {
  },
};

return obj;

// bad
const arr = [
  function foo() {
  },
  function bar() {
  },
];
return arr;

// good
const arr = [
  function foo() {
  },

  function bar() {
  },
];

return arr;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

  <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

  <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--padded-blocks"></a><a name="user-content-18.8"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--padded-blocks">19.8</a> Do not pad your blocks with blank lines. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/padded-blocks.html" rel="nofollow"><code>padded-blocks</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function bar() {

  console.log(foo);

}

// bad
if (baz) {

  console.log(qux);
} else {
  console.log(foo);

}

// bad
class Foo {

  constructor(bar) {
    this.bar = bar;
  }
}

// good
function bar() {
  console.log(foo);
}

// good
if (baz) {
  console.log(qux);
} else {
  console.log(foo);
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>

  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">qux</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">qux</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--no-multiple-blanks"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--no-multiple-blanks">19.9</a> Do not use multiple blank lines to pad your code. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-multiple-empty-lines" rel="nofollow"><code>no-multiple-empty-lines</code></a></p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
class Person {
  constructor(fullName, email, birthday) {
    this.fullName = fullName;


    this.email = email;


    this.setAge(birthday);
  }


  setAge(birthday) {
    const today = new Date();


    const age = this.getAge(today, birthday);


    this.age = age;
  }


  getAge(today, birthday) {
    // ..
  }
}

// good
class Person {
  constructor(fullName, email, birthday) {
    this.fullName = fullName;
    this.email = email;
    this.setAge(birthday);
  }

  setAge(birthday) {
    const today = new Date();
    const age = getAge(today, birthday);
    this.age = age;
  }

  getAge(today, birthday) {
    // ..
  }
}

  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">fullName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">email</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">birthday</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>


  <span class="pl-en">getAge</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">today</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">birthday</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// ..</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Person</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">fullName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">email</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">birthday</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">fullName</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">fullName</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">email</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">email</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">setAge</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">birthday</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">today</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Date</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">age</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">getAge</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">today</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">birthday</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--in-parens"></a><a name="user-content-18.9"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--in-parens">19.10</a> Do not add spaces inside parentheses. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/space-in-parens.html" rel="nofollow"><code>space-in-parens</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function bar( foo ) {
  return foo;
}

// good
function bar(foo) {
  return foo;
}

// bad
if ( foo ) {
  console.log(foo);
}

// good
if (foo) {
  console.log(foo);
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--in-brackets"></a><a name="user-content-18.10"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--in-brackets">19.11</a> Do not add spaces inside brackets. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/array-bracket-spacing.html" rel="nofollow"><code>array-bracket-spacing</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const foo = [ 1, 2, 3 ];
console.log(foo[ 0 ]);

// good
const foo = [1, 2, 3];
console.log(foo[0]);
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span> <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--in-braces"></a><a name="user-content-18.11"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--in-braces">19.12</a> Add spaces inside curly braces. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/object-curly-spacing.html" rel="nofollow"><code>object-curly-spacing</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const foo = {clark: 'kent'};

// good
const foo = { clark: 'kent' };
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">clark</span>: <span class="pl-s">'kent'</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">clark</span>: <span class="pl-s">'kent'</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--max-len"></a><a name="user-content-18.12"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--max-len">19.13</a> Avoid having lines of code that are longer than 100 characters (including whitespace). Note: per <a href="#strings--line-length">above</a>, long strings are exempt from this rule, and should not be broken up. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/max-len.html" rel="nofollow"><code>max-len</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? This ensures readability and maintainability.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const foo = jsonData &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo.bar &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo.bar.baz &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo.bar.baz.quux &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo.bar.baz.quux.xyzzy;

// bad
$.ajax({ method: 'POST', url: 'https://airbnb.com/', data: { name: 'John' } }).done(() =&gt; console.log('Congratulations!')).fail(() =&gt; console.log('You have failed this city.'));

// good
const foo = jsonData
  &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo
  &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo.bar
  &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo.bar.baz
  &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo.bar.baz.quux
  &amp;&amp; jsonData.foo.bar.baz.quux.xyzzy;

// good
$.ajax({
  method: 'POST',
  url: 'https://airbnb.com/',
  data: { name: 'John' },
})
  .done(() =&gt; console.log('Congratulations!'))
  .fail(() =&gt; console.log('You have failed this city.'));
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">baz</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">quux</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">quux</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">xyzzy</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
