<span class="pl-s1">$</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">ajax</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">method</span>: <span class="pl-s">'POST'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">url</span>: <span class="pl-s">'https://airbnb.com/'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">'John'</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">done</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Congratulations!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">fail</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'You have failed this city.'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">baz</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">quux</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jsonData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">baz</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">quux</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">xyzzy</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-s1">$</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">ajax</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">method</span>: <span class="pl-s">'POST'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">url</span>: <span class="pl-s">'https://airbnb.com/'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">'John'</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">done</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Congratulations!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">fail</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'You have failed this city.'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--block-spacing"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--block-spacing">19.14</a> Require consistent spacing inside an open block token and the next token on the same line. This rule also enforces consistent spacing inside a close block token and previous token on the same line. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/block-spacing" rel="nofollow"><code>block-spacing</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function foo() {return true;}
if (foo) { bar = 0;}

// good
function foo() { return true; }
if (foo) { bar = 0; }
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--comma-spacing"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--comma-spacing">19.15</a> Avoid spaces before commas and require a space after commas. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/comma-spacing" rel="nofollow"><code>comma-spacing</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
var foo = 1,bar = 2;
var arr = [1 , 2];

// good
var foo = 1, bar = 2;
var arr = [1, 2];
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span><span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">arr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--computed-property-spacing"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--computed-property-spacing">19.16</a> Enforce spacing inside of computed property brackets. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/computed-property-spacing" rel="nofollow"><code>computed-property-spacing</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
obj[foo ]
obj[ 'foo']
var x = {[ b ]: a}
obj[foo[ bar ]]

// good
obj[foo]
obj['foo']
var x = { [b]: a }
obj[foo[bar]]
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span> <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span> <span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span> <span class="pl-s1">b</span> <span class="pl-kos">]</span>: <span class="pl-s1">a</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span> <span class="pl-s1">bar</span> <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s">'foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">b</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span>: <span class="pl-s1">a</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-s1">obj</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">bar</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--func-call-spacing"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--func-call-spacing">19.17</a> Avoid spaces between functions and their invocations. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/func-call-spacing" rel="nofollow"><code>func-call-spacing</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
func ();

func
();

// good
func();
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-en">func</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-en">func</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-en">func</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--key-spacing"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--key-spacing">19.18</a> Enforce spacing between keys and values in object literal properties. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/key-spacing" rel="nofollow"><code>key-spacing</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
var obj = { foo : 42 };
var obj2 = { foo:42 };

// good
var obj = { foo: 42 };
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">foo</span> : <span class="pl-c1">42</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj2</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">foo</span>:<span class="pl-c1">42</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">obj</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">foo</span>: <span class="pl-c1">42</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--no-trailing-spaces"></a></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#whitespace--no-trailing-spaces">19.19</a> Avoid trailing spaces at the end of lines. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-trailing-spaces" rel="nofollow"><code>no-trailing-spaces</code></a></li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-whitespace--no-multiple-empty-lines"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#whitespace--no-multiple-empty-lines">19.20</a> Avoid multiple empty lines, only allow one newline at the end of files, and avoid a newline at the beginning of files. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-multiple-empty-lines" rel="nofollow"><code>no-multiple-empty-lines</code></a></p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad - multiple empty lines
var x = 1;


var y = 2;

// bad - 2+ newlines at end of file
var x = 1;
var y = 2;


// bad - 1+ newline(s) at beginning of file

var x = 1;
var y = 2;

// good
var x = 1;
var y = 2;

"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad - multiple empty lines</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>


<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad - 2+ newlines at end of file</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>


<span class="pl-c">// bad - 1+ newline(s) at beginning of file</span>

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>

</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-commas" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#commas"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Commas</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-commas--leading-trailing"></a><a name="user-content-19.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#commas--leading-trailing">20.1</a> Leading commas: <strong>Nope.</strong> eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/comma-style.html" rel="nofollow"><code>comma-style</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const story = [
    once
  , upon
  , aTime
];

// good
const story = [
  once,
  upon,
  aTime,
];

// bad
const hero = {
    firstName: 'Ada'
  , lastName: 'Lovelace'
  , birthYear: 1815
  , superPower: 'computers'
};

// good
const hero = {
  firstName: 'Ada',
  lastName: 'Lovelace',
  birthYear: 1815,
  superPower: 'computers',
};
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">story</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">once</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">upon</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">aTime</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">story</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">once</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">upon</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">aTime</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">hero</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">firstName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Ada'</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">lastName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Lovelace'</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">birthYear</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1815</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">superPower</span>: <span class="pl-s">'computers'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">hero</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">firstName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Ada'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">lastName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Lovelace'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">birthYear</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1815</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">superPower</span>: <span class="pl-s">'computers'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-commas--dangling"></a><a name="user-content-19.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#commas--dangling">20.2</a> Additional trailing comma: <strong>Yup.</strong> eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/comma-dangle.html" rel="nofollow"><code>comma-dangle</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? This leads to cleaner git diffs. Also, transpilers like Babel will remove the additional trailing comma in the transpiled code which means you don’t have to worry about the <a href="https://github.com/airbnb/javascript/blob/es5-deprecated/es5/README.md#commas">trailing comma problem</a> in legacy browsers.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-diff position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad - git diff without trailing comma
const hero = {
     firstName: 'Florence',
-    lastName: 'Nightingale'
+    lastName: 'Nightingale',
+    inventorOf: ['coxcomb chart', 'modern nursing']
};

// good - git diff with trailing comma
const hero = {
     firstName: 'Florence',
     lastName: 'Nightingale',
+    inventorOf: ['coxcomb chart', 'modern nursing'],
};
"><pre>// bad - git diff without trailing comma
const hero = {
     firstName: 'Florence',
<span class="pl-md"><span class="pl-md">-</span>    lastName: 'Nightingale'</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>    lastName: 'Nightingale',</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>    inventorOf: ['coxcomb chart', 'modern nursing']</span>
};

// good - git diff with trailing comma
const hero = {
     firstName: 'Florence',
     lastName: 'Nightingale',
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>    inventorOf: ['coxcomb chart', 'modern nursing'],</span>
};</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const hero = {
  firstName: 'Dana',
  lastName: 'Scully'
};

const heroes = [
  'Batman',
  'Superman'
];

// good
const hero = {
  firstName: 'Dana',
  lastName: 'Scully',
};

const heroes = [
  'Batman',
  'Superman',
];

// bad
function createHero(
  firstName,
  lastName,
  inventorOf
) {
  // does nothing
}

// good
function createHero(
  firstName,
  lastName,
  inventorOf,
) {
  // does nothing
}

// good (note that a comma must not appear after a &quot;rest&quot; element)
function createHero(
  firstName,
  lastName,
  inventorOf,
  ...heroArgs
) {
  // does nothing
}

// bad
createHero(
  firstName,
  lastName,
  inventorOf
);

// good
createHero(
  firstName,
  lastName,
  inventorOf,
);

// good (note that a comma must not appear after a &quot;rest&quot; element)
createHero(
  firstName,
  lastName,
  inventorOf,
  ...heroArgs
);
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">hero</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">firstName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Dana'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">lastName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Scully'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">heroes</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'Batman'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'Superman'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">hero</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">firstName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Dana'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">lastName</span>: <span class="pl-s">'Scully'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">heroes</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'Batman'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">'Superman'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">createHero</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">inventorOf</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// does nothing</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">createHero</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">inventorOf</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// does nothing</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good (note that a comma must not appear after a "rest" element)</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">createHero</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">inventorOf</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  ...<span class="pl-s1">heroArgs</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// does nothing</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-en">createHero</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">inventorOf</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-en">createHero</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">inventorOf</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good (note that a comma must not appear after a "rest" element)</span>
<span class="pl-en">createHero</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">firstName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">lastName</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">inventorOf</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  ...<span class="pl-s1">heroArgs</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-semicolons" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#semicolons"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Semicolons</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-semicolons--required"></a><a name="user-content-20.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#semicolons--required">21.1</a> <strong>Yup.</strong> eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/semi.html" rel="nofollow"><code>semi</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? When JavaScript encounters a line break without a semicolon, it uses a set of rules called <a href="https://tc39.github.io/ecma262/#sec-automatic-semicolon-insertion" rel="nofollow">Automatic Semicolon Insertion</a> to determine whether it should regard that line break as the end of a statement, and (as the name implies) place a semicolon into your code before the line break if it thinks so. ASI contains a few eccentric behaviors, though, and your code will break if JavaScript misinterprets your line break. These rules will become more complicated as new features become a part of JavaScript. Explicitly terminating your statements and configuring your linter to catch missing semicolons will help prevent you from encountering issues.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad - raises exception
const luke = {}
const leia = {}
[luke, leia].forEach((jedi) =&gt; jedi.father = 'vader')

// bad - raises exception
const reaction = &quot;No! That’s impossible!&quot;
(async function meanwhileOnTheFalcon() {
  // handle `leia`, `lando`, `chewie`, `r2`, `c3p0`
  // ...
}())

// bad - returns `undefined` instead of the value on the next line - always happens when `return` is on a line by itself because of ASI!
function foo() {
  return
    'search your feelings, you know it to be foo'
}

// good
const luke = {};
const leia = {};
[luke, leia].forEach((jedi) =&gt; {
  jedi.father = 'vader';
});

// good
const reaction = &quot;No! That’s impossible!&quot;;
(async function meanwhileOnTheFalcon() {
  // handle `leia`, `lando`, `chewie`, `r2`, `c3p0`
  // ...
}());

// good
function foo() {
  return 'search your feelings, you know it to be foo';
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad - raises exception</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">luke</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">leia</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">luke</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">leia</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">forEach</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">jedi</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">jedi</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">father</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'vader'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad - raises exception</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">reaction</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"No! That’s impossible!"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">meanwhileOnTheFalcon</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// handle `leia`, `lando`, `chewie`, `r2`, `c3p0`</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad - returns `undefined` instead of the value on the next line - always happens when `return` is on a line by itself because of ASI!</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span>
    <span class="pl-s">'search your feelings, you know it to be foo'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">luke</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">leia</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">luke</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">leia</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">forEach</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">jedi</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">jedi</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">father</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'vader'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">reaction</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"No! That’s impossible!"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">meanwhileOnTheFalcon</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// handle `leia`, `lando`, `chewie`, `r2`, `c3p0`</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">'search your feelings, you know it to be foo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p><a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/7365172/semicolon-before-self-invoking-function/7365214#7365214" rel="nofollow">Read more</a>.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-type-casting--coercion" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#type-casting--coercion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Type Casting &amp; Coercion</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-coercion--explicit"></a><a name="user-content-21.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#coercion--explicit">22.1</a> Perform type coercion at the beginning of the statement.</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-coercion--strings"></a><a name="user-content-21.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#coercion--strings">22.2</a> Strings: eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-new-wrappers" rel="nofollow"><code>no-new-wrappers</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// =&gt; this.reviewScore = 9;

// bad
const totalScore = new String(this.reviewScore); // typeof totalScore is &quot;object&quot; not &quot;string&quot;

// bad
const totalScore = this.reviewScore + ''; // invokes this.reviewScore.valueOf()

// bad
const totalScore = this.reviewScore.toString(); // isn’t guaranteed to return a string

// good
const totalScore = String(this.reviewScore);
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// =&gt; this.reviewScore = 9;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">totalScore</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">String</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">reviewScore</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// typeof totalScore is "object" not "string"</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">totalScore</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">reviewScore</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s">''</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// invokes this.reviewScore.valueOf()</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">totalScore</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">reviewScore</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">toString</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// isn’t guaranteed to return a string</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">totalScore</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">String</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">reviewScore</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-coercion--numbers"></a><a name="user-content-21.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#coercion--numbers">22.3</a> Numbers: Use <code>Number</code> for type casting and <code>parseInt</code> always with a radix for parsing strings. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/radix" rel="nofollow"><code>radix</code></a> <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-new-wrappers" rel="nofollow"><code>no-new-wrappers</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? The <code>parseInt</code> function produces an integer value dictated by interpretation of the contents of the string argument according to the specified radix. Leading whitespace in string is ignored. If radix is <code>undefined</code> or <code>0</code>, it is assumed to be <code>10</code> except when the number begins with the character pairs <code>0x</code> or <code>0X</code>, in which case a radix of 16 is assumed. This differs from ECMAScript 3, which merely discouraged (but allowed) octal interpretation. Many implementations have not adopted this behavior as of 2013. And, because older browsers must be supported, always specify a radix.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const inputValue = '4';

// bad
const val = new Number(inputValue);

// bad
const val = +inputValue;

// bad
const val = inputValue &gt;&gt; 0;

// bad
const val = parseInt(inputValue);

// good
const val = Number(inputValue);

// good
const val = parseInt(inputValue, 10);
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">inputValue</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'4'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Number</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">inputValue</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span><span class="pl-s1">inputValue</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">inputValue</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">parseInt</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">inputValue</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Number</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">inputValue</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">parseInt</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">inputValue</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-coercion--comment-deviations"></a><a name="user-content-21.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#coercion--comment-deviations">22.4</a> If for whatever reason you are doing something wild and <code>parseInt</code> is your bottleneck and need to use Bitshift for <a href="https://jsperf.com/coercion-vs-casting/3" rel="nofollow">performance reasons</a>, leave a comment explaining why and what you’re doing.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// good
/**
 * parseInt was the reason my code was slow.
 * Bitshifting the String to coerce it to a
 * Number made it a lot faster.
 */
const val = inputValue &gt;&gt; 0;
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c"> * parseInt was the reason my code was slow.</span>
<span class="pl-c"> * Bitshifting the String to coerce it to a</span>
<span class="pl-c"> * Number made it a lot faster.</span>
<span class="pl-c"> */</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">inputValue</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-coercion--bitwise"></a><a name="user-content-21.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#coercion--bitwise">22.5</a> <strong>Note:</strong> Be careful when using bitshift operations. Numbers are represented as <a href="https://es5.github.io/#x4.3.19" rel="nofollow">64-bit values</a>, but bitshift operations always return a 32-bit integer (<a href="https://es5.github.io/#x11.7" rel="nofollow">source</a>). Bitshift can lead to unexpected behavior for integer values larger than 32 bits. <a href="https://github.com/airbnb/javascript/issues/109">Discussion</a>. Largest signed 32-bit Int is 2,147,483,647:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="2147483647 &gt;&gt; 0; // =&gt; 2147483647
2147483648 &gt;&gt; 0; // =&gt; -2147483648
2147483649 &gt;&gt; 0; // =&gt; -2147483647
"><pre><span class="pl-c1">2147483647</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; 2147483647</span>
<span class="pl-c1">2147483648</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; -2147483648</span>
<span class="pl-c1">2147483649</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// =&gt; -2147483647</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-coercion--booleans"></a><a name="user-content-21.6"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#coercion--booleans">22.6</a> Booleans: eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-new-wrappers" rel="nofollow"><code>no-new-wrappers</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const age = 0;

// bad
const hasAge = new Boolean(age);

// good
const hasAge = Boolean(age);

// best
const hasAge = !!age;
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">age</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">hasAge</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Boolean</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">age</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">hasAge</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Boolean</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">age</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">hasAge</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">age</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-naming-conventions" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#naming-conventions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Naming Conventions</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--descriptive"></a><a name="user-content-22.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--descriptive">23.1</a> Avoid single letter names. Be descriptive with your naming. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/id-length" rel="nofollow"><code>id-length</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function q() {
  // ...
}

// good
function query() {
  // ...
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">q</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">query</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--camelcase"></a><a name="user-content-22.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--camelCase">23.2</a> Use camelCase when naming objects, functions, and instances. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/camelcase.html" rel="nofollow"><code>camelcase</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const OBJEcttsssss = {};
const this_is_my_object = {};
function c() {}

// good
const thisIsMyObject = {};
function thisIsMyFunction() {}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">OBJEcttsssss</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">this_is_my_object</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">c</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">thisIsMyObject</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">thisIsMyFunction</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--pascalcase"></a><a name="user-content-22.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--PascalCase">23.3</a> Use PascalCase only when naming constructors or classes. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/new-cap.html" rel="nofollow"><code>new-cap</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function user(options) {
  this.name = options.name;
}

const bad = new user({
  name: 'nope',
});

// good
class User {
  constructor(options) {
    this.name = options.name;
  }
}

const good = new User({
  name: 'yup',
});
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">user</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">options</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">options</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">bad</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-s1">user</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">'nope'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">User</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">options</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">options</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">good</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">User</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">'yup'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--leading-underscore"></a><a name="user-content-22.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--leading-underscore">23.4</a> Do not use trailing or leading underscores. eslint: <a href="https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-underscore-dangle.html" rel="nofollow"><code>no-underscore-dangle</code></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? JavaScript does not have the concept of privacy in terms of properties or methods. Although a leading underscore is a common convention to mean “private”, in fact, these properties are fully public, and as such, are part of your public API contract. This convention might lead developers to wrongly think that a change won’t count as breaking, or that tests aren’t needed. tl;dr: if you want something to be “private”, it must not be observably present.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
this.__firstName__ = 'Panda';
this.firstName_ = 'Panda';
this._firstName = 'Panda';

// good
this.firstName = 'Panda';

// good, in environments where WeakMaps are available
// see https://kangax.github.io/compat-table/es6/#test-WeakMap
const firstNames = new WeakMap();
firstNames.set(this, 'Panda');
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">__firstName__</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Panda'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">firstName_</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Panda'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">_firstName</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Panda'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">firstName</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Panda'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good, in environments where WeakMaps are available</span>
<span class="pl-c">// see https://kangax.github.io/compat-table/es6/#test-WeakMap</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">firstNames</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">WeakMap</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">firstNames</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">set</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">'Panda'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--self-this"></a><a name="user-content-22.5"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--self-this">23.5</a> Don’t save references to <code>this</code>. Use arrow functions or <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Function/bind" rel="nofollow">Function#bind</a>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
function foo() {
  const self = this;
  return function () {
    console.log(self);
  };
}

// bad
function foo() {
  const that = this;
  return function () {
    console.log(that);
  };
}

// good
function foo() {
  return () =&gt; {
    console.log(this);
  };
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">self</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">that</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">that</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--filename-matches-export"></a><a name="user-content-22.6"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--filename-matches-export">23.6</a> A base filename should exactly match the name of its default export.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// file 1 contents
class CheckBox {
  // ...
}
export default CheckBox;

// file 2 contents
export default function fortyTwo() { return 42; }

// file 3 contents
export default function insideDirectory() {}

// in some other file
// bad
import CheckBox from './checkBox'; // PascalCase import/export, camelCase filename
import FortyTwo from './FortyTwo'; // PascalCase import/filename, camelCase export
import InsideDirectory from './InsideDirectory'; // PascalCase import/filename, camelCase export

// bad
import CheckBox from './check_box'; // PascalCase import/export, snake_case filename
import forty_two from './forty_two'; // snake_case import/filename, camelCase export
import inside_directory from './inside_directory'; // snake_case import, camelCase export
import index from './inside_directory/index'; // requiring the index file explicitly
import insideDirectory from './insideDirectory/index'; // requiring the index file explicitly

// good
import CheckBox from './CheckBox'; // PascalCase export/import/filename
import fortyTwo from './fortyTwo'; // camelCase export/import/filename
import insideDirectory from './insideDirectory'; // camelCase export/import/directory name/implicit &quot;index&quot;
// ^ supports both insideDirectory.js and insideDirectory/index.js
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// file 1 contents</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">CheckBox</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-v">CheckBox</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// file 2 contents</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">fortyTwo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">42</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// file 3 contents</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">insideDirectory</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// in some other file</span>
<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">CheckBox</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./checkBox'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// PascalCase import/export, camelCase filename</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">FortyTwo</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./FortyTwo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// PascalCase import/filename, camelCase export</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">InsideDirectory</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./InsideDirectory'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// PascalCase import/filename, camelCase export</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">CheckBox</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./check_box'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// PascalCase import/export, snake_case filename</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">forty_two</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./forty_two'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// snake_case import/filename, camelCase export</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">inside_directory</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./inside_directory'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// snake_case import, camelCase export</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">index</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./inside_directory/index'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// requiring the index file explicitly</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">insideDirectory</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./insideDirectory/index'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// requiring the index file explicitly</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">CheckBox</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./CheckBox'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// PascalCase export/import/filename</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">fortyTwo</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./fortyTwo'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// camelCase export/import/filename</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">insideDirectory</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./insideDirectory'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// camelCase export/import/directory name/implicit "index"</span>
<span class="pl-c">// ^ supports both insideDirectory.js and insideDirectory/index.js</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--camelcase-default-export"></a><a name="user-content-22.7"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--camelCase-default-export">23.7</a> Use camelCase when you export-default a function. Your filename should be identical to your function’s name.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="function makeStyleGuide() {
  // ...
}

export default makeStyleGuide;
"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">makeStyleGuide</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-s1">makeStyleGuide</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--pascalcase-singleton"></a><a name="user-content-22.8"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--PascalCase-singleton">23.8</a> Use PascalCase when you export a constructor / class / singleton / function library / bare object.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const AirbnbStyleGuide = {
  es6: {
  },
};

export default AirbnbStyleGuide;
"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">AirbnbStyleGuide</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">es6</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-v">AirbnbStyleGuide</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--acronyms-and-initialisms"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--Acronyms-and-Initialisms">23.9</a> Acronyms and initialisms should always be all uppercased, or all lowercased.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? Names are for readability, not to appease a computer algorithm.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
import SmsContainer from './containers/SmsContainer';

// bad
const HttpRequests = [
  // ...
];

// good
import SMSContainer from './containers/SMSContainer';

// good
const HTTPRequests = [
  // ...
];

// also good
const httpRequests = [
  // ...
];

// best
import TextMessageContainer from './containers/TextMessageContainer';

// best
const requests = [
  // ...
];
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">SmsContainer</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./containers/SmsContainer'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">HttpRequests</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">SMSContainer</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./containers/SMSContainer'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">HTTPRequests</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// also good</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">httpRequests</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">TextMessageContainer</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">'./containers/TextMessageContainer'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// best</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-naming--uppercase"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#naming--uppercase">23.10</a> You may optionally uppercase a constant only if it (1) is exported, (2) is a <code>const</code> (it can not be reassigned), and (3) the programmer can trust it (and its nested properties) to never change.</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Why? This is an additional tool to assist in situations where the programmer would be unsure if a variable might ever change. UPPERCASE_VARIABLES are letting the programmer know that they can trust the variable (and its properties) not to change.</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>What about all <code>const</code> variables? - This is unnecessary, so uppercasing should not be used for constants within a file. It should be used for exported constants however.</li>
<li>What about exported objects? - Uppercase at the top level of export (e.g. <code>EXPORTED_OBJECT.key</code>) and maintain that all nested properties do not change.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
const PRIVATE_VARIABLE = 'should not be unnecessarily uppercased within a file';

// bad
export const THING_TO_BE_CHANGED = 'should obviously not be uppercased';

// bad
export let REASSIGNABLE_VARIABLE = 'do not use let with uppercase variables';

// ---

// allowed but does not supply semantic value
export const apiKey = 'SOMEKEY';

// better in most cases
export const API_KEY = 'SOMEKEY';

// ---

// bad - unnecessarily uppercases key while adding no semantic value
export const MAPPING = {
  KEY: 'value'
};

// good
export const MAPPING = {
  key: 'value'
};
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-c1">PRIVATE_VARIABLE</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'should not be unnecessarily uppercased within a file'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-c1">THING_TO_BE_CHANGED</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'should obviously not be uppercased'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-c1">REASSIGNABLE_VARIABLE</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'do not use let with uppercase variables'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ---</span>

<span class="pl-c">// allowed but does not supply semantic value</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">apiKey</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'SOMEKEY'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// better in most cases</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-c1">API_KEY</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'SOMEKEY'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ---</span>

<span class="pl-c">// bad - unnecessarily uppercases key while adding no semantic value</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-c1">MAPPING</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">KEY</span>: <span class="pl-s">'value'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-c1">MAPPING</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">key</span>: <span class="pl-s">'value'</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-accessors" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#accessors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Accessors</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-accessors--not-required"></a><a name="user-content-23.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#accessors--not-required">24.1</a> Accessor functions for properties are not required.</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-accessors--no-getters-setters"></a><a name="user-content-23.2"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#accessors--no-getters-setters">24.2</a> Do not use JavaScript getters/setters as they cause unexpected side effects and are harder to test, maintain, and reason about. Instead, if you do make accessor functions, use <code>getVal()</code> and <code>setVal('hello')</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
class Dragon {
  get age() {
    // ...
  }

  set age(value) {
    // ...
  }
}

// good
class Dragon {
  getAge() {
    // ...
  }

  setAge(value) {
    // ...
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Dragon</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">get</span> <span class="pl-en">age</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-k">set</span> <span class="pl-en">age</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Dragon</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">getAge</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">setAge</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">value</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-accessors--boolean-prefix"></a><a name="user-content-23.3"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#accessors--boolean-prefix">24.3</a> If the property/method is a <code>boolean</code>, use <code>isVal()</code> or <code>hasVal()</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
if (!dragon.age()) {
  return false;
}

// good
if (!dragon.hasAge()) {
  return false;
}
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">dragon</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">age</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">dragon</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">hasAge</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a name="user-content-accessors--consistent"></a><a name="user-content-23.4"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#accessors--consistent">24.4</a> It’s okay to create <code>get()</code> and <code>set()</code> functions, but be consistent.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="class Jedi {
  constructor(options = {}) {
    const lightsaber = options.lightsaber || 'blue';
    this.set('lightsaber', lightsaber);
  }

  set(key, val) {
    this[key] = val;
  }

  get(key) {
    return this[key];
  }
}
"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Jedi</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-en">constructor</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">options</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">lightsaber</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">options</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">lightsaber</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s">'blue'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">set</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'lightsaber'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">lightsaber</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">set</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><a href="#table-of-contents"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="arrow_up" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2b06.png">⬆</g-emoji> back to top</a></strong></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-events" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#events"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Events</h2>
<p><a name="user-content-events--hash"></a><a name="user-content-24.1"></a></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><a href="#events--hash">25.1</a> When attaching data payloads to events (whether DOM events or something more proprietary like Backbone events), pass an object literal (also known as a "hash") instead of a raw value. This allows a subsequent contributor to add more data to the event payload without finding and updating every handler for the event. For example, instead of:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// bad
$(this).trigger('listingUpdated', listing.id);

// ...

$(this).on('listingUpdated', (e, listingID) =&gt; {
  // do something with listingID
});
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// bad</span>
<span class="pl-en">$</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">trigger</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'listingUpdated'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">listing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ...</span>

<span class="pl-en">$</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'listingUpdated'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">e</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">listingID</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// do something with listingID</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p>prefer:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// good
$(this).trigger('listingUpdated', { listingID: listing.id });

// ...

$(this).on('listingUpdated', (e, data) =&gt; {
  // do something with data.listingID
});
"><pre><span class="pl-c">// good</span>
<span class="pl-en">$</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">trigger</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'listingUpdated'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">listingID</span>: <span class="pl-s1">listing</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">id</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ...</span>

<span class="pl-en">$</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'listingUpdated'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">e</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// do something with data.listingID</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
